            <div class="provider-chips" id="providerChips">
                <div class="provider-chip" data-provider="mtn_momo" onclick="selectProvider('mtn_momo',this)">MTN MoMo</div>
                <div class="provider-chip" data-provider="vodafone_cash" onclick="selectProvider('vodafone_cash',this)">Vodafone Cash</div>
            </div>
            <div class="form-group" style="margin-bottom:20px;">
                <label style="display:block;font-family:'Space Grotesk',sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:#334155;margin-bottom:7px;">Phone Number</label>
                <input style="width:100%;padding:14px 16px;font-family:'DM Sans',sans-serif;font-size:16px;color:#334155;background:#fafaf9;border:2px solid #e2e8f0;border-radius:12px;outline:none;" type="tel" id="payPhone" placeholder="Collector's phone">
            </div>
            <div class="pay-actions">
                <button class="btn-pay-confirm btn-cancel" onclick="closePayModal()">Cancel</button>
                <button class="btn-pay-confirm btn-confirm" id="payConfirmBtn" onclick="confirmPayment()" disabled>Send Payment</button>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
    (function() {
        'use strict';

        var MATERIAL_COLORS = { PET: '#16a34a', HDPE: '#3b82f6', LDPE: '#f59e0b', PP: '#ef4444' };

        var state = {
            operator: null,
            stats: null,
            collections: [],
            collectionsTotal: 0,
            collectionsOffset: 0,
            collectionsLimit: 25,
            sortField: 'transaction_date',
            sortDir: 'desc',
            materialFilter: '',
            refreshTimer: null,
            refreshInterval: 30000
        };

        // ---- AUTH ----
        var ROLE_ROUTES = {
            collector: '/collector-dashboard',
            aggregator: '/aggregator-dashboard',
            processor: '/processor-dashboard',
            converter: '/converter-dashboard'
        };

        function checkAuth() {
            var saved = localStorage.getItem('circul_operator');
            if (saved) {
                try {
                    state.operator = JSON.parse(saved);
                    var route = ROLE_ROUTES[state.operator.role];
                    if (route) { window.location.href = route; return; }
                    showDashboard();
                    return;
                } catch (e) {
                    localStorage.removeItem('circul_operator');
                }
            }
            showLogin();
        }

        function showLogin() {
            document.getElementById('loginOverlay').classList.remove('hidden');
        }

        function showDashboard() {
            document.getElementById('loginOverlay').classList.add('hidden');
            var op = state.operator;
            document.getElementById('navUser').style.display = 'flex';
            document.getElementById('navUserName').textContent = op.name + (op.company ? ' (' + op.company + ')' : '');
            var badge = document.getElementById('navRoleBadge');
            badge.textContent = op.role;
            badge.className = 'role-badge ' + op.role;
            document.getElementById('logoutBtn').style.display = '';

            if (op.role === 'admin') {
                document.getElementById('navTitle').textContent = 'Admin Dashboard — All Operators';
            } else {
                document.getElementById('navTitle').textContent = op.company || op.name;
            }

            loadAll();
        }

        window.handleOperatorLogin = function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var phone = document.getElementById('loginPhone').value.trim();
            var pin = document.getElementById('loginPin').value.trim();
            if (!phone || !pin) return;

            var btn = document.getElementById('loginBtn');
            btn.disabled = true; btn.innerHTML = '<div class="spinner"></div>';
            document.getElementById('loginError').classList.remove('visible');

            fetch('/api/operators/login', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ phone: phone, pin: pin })
            })
            .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
            .then(function(data) {
                if (data.success) {
                    state.operator = data.operator;
                    localStorage.setItem('circul_operator', JSON.stringify(data.operator));
                    var route = ROLE_ROUTES[data.operator.role];
                    if (route) { window.location.href = route; return; }
                    showDashboard();
                } else {
                    var errEl = document.getElementById('loginError');
                    errEl.textContent = data.message || 'Invalid phone or PIN';
                    errEl.classList.add('visible');
                }
            })
            .catch(function() {
                var errEl = document.getElementById('loginError');
                errEl.textContent = 'Connection error. Please try again.';
                errEl.classList.add('visible');
            })
            .finally(function() {
                btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'Log In';
            });
        };

        window.handleLogout = function() {
            state.operator = null;
            localStorage.removeItem('circul_operator');
            if (state.refreshTimer) clearInterval(state.refreshTimer);
            document.getElementById('navUser').style.display = 'none';
            document.getElementById('logoutBtn').style.display = 'none';
            showLogin();
        };

        // ---- API ----
        function getOperatorParam() {
            if (state.operator && state.operator.role !== 'admin') {
                return 'operator_id=' + state.operator.id;
            }
            return '';
        }

        function fetchJSON(url) {
            return fetch(url).then(function(r) {
                if (!r.ok) throw new Error('HTTP ' + r.status);
                return r.json();
            });
        }

        function loadStats() {
            var params = getOperatorParam();
            return fetchJSON('/api/stats' + (params ? '?' + params : '')).then(function(data) {
                if (data.success) {
                    state.stats = data.stats;
                    renderStatsCards(); renderMaterialBreakdown(); renderLeaderboard(); renderTrendChart();
                }
            }).catch(function(err) { console.error('Stats error:', err); });
        }

        function loadCollections() {
            var params = new URLSearchParams();
            params.set('limit', state.collectionsLimit);
            params.set('offset', state.collectionsOffset);
            if (state.materialFilter) params.set('material_type', state.materialFilter);
            if (state.operator && state.operator.role !== 'admin') params.set('operator_id', state.operator.id);

            return fetchJSON('/api/transactions?' + params.toString()).then(function(data) {
                if (data.success) {
                    state.collections = data.transactions;
                    state.collectionsTotal = data.total;
                    sortLocal(); renderCollections();
                }
            }).catch(function(err) {
                console.error('Transactions error:', err);
                document.getElementById('collectionsBody').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="table-empty" style="color:var(--red)">Failed to load</td></tr>';
            });
        }

        function loadAll() {
            Promise.all([loadStats(), loadCollections()]).then(function() { resetRefreshTimer(); });
        }

        // ---- RENDER ----
        function formatNum(n) {
            if (n == null || isNaN(n)) return '0';
            var num = parseFloat(n);
            if (num >= 10000) return num.toLocaleString('en-US', { maximumFractionDigits: 0 });
            if (num >= 100) return num.toLocaleString('en-US', { maximumFractionDigits: 1 });
            return num.toLocaleString('en-US', { maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
        }

        function renderStatsCards() {
            var s = state.stats; if (!s) return;
            document.getElementById('statTotalWeight').textContent = formatNum(s.totals.total_weight_kg);
            document.getElementById('statTotalCollections').textContent = formatNum(s.totals.total_transactions);
            document.getElementById('statActivePickers').textContent = formatNum(s.totals.active_collectors);
            document.getElementById('statTodayWeight').textContent = formatNum(s.today.today_weight_kg);
            document.getElementById('statTodayCount').textContent = formatNum(s.today.today_transactions) + ' transactions today';
        }

        function renderMaterialBreakdown() {
            var materials = state.stats ? state.stats.by_material : [];
            var c = document.getElementById('materialBreakdown');
            if (!materials || !materials.length) { c.innerHTML = '<div class="table-empty">No data yet</div>'; return; }
            var totalKg = materials.reduce(function(s, m) { return s + parseFloat(m.total_kg); }, 0);
            var maxKg = parseFloat(materials[0].total_kg);
            var html = '';
            materials.forEach(function(m) {
                var kg = parseFloat(m.total_kg);
                var pct = totalKg > 0 ? (kg / totalKg * 100) : 0;
                var bw = maxKg > 0 ? (kg / maxKg * 100) : 0;
                var color = MATERIAL_COLORS[m.material_type] || '#6b7280';
                html += '<div class="material-row"><span class="material-label">' + esc(m.material_type) + '</span><div class="material-bar-track"><div class="material-bar-fill" style="width:' + bw.toFixed(1) + '%;background:' + color + '"></div></div><span class="material-kg">' + formatNum(kg) + ' kg</span><span class="material-pct">' + pct.toFixed(1) + '%</span></div>';
            });
            c.innerHTML = html;
        }

        function renderLeaderboard() {
            var collectors = state.stats ? state.stats.top_collectors : [];
            var c = document.getElementById('leaderboard');
            if (!collectors || !collectors.length) { c.innerHTML = '<div class="table-empty">No data yet</div>'; return; }
            var html = '';
            collectors.forEach(function(col, i) {
                var rank = i + 1;
                var bc = rank === 1 ? 'gold' : rank === 2 ? 'silver' : rank === 3 ? 'bronze' : 'default';
                var name = col.first_name + (col.last_name ? ' ' + col.last_name : '');
                var rating = col.average_rating ? ' ⭐ ' + parseFloat(col.average_rating).toFixed(1) : '';
                html += '<div class="leaderboard-item"><div class="rank-badge ' + bc + '">' + rank + '</div><div class="leaderboard-info"><div class="leaderboard-name">' + esc(name) + rating + '</div><div class="leaderboard-meta">' + formatNum(col.transactions) + ' txns</div></div><div class="leaderboard-kg">' + formatNum(col.total_kg) + ' kg</div></div>';
            });
            c.innerHTML = html;
        }

        function renderTrendChart() {
            var trend = state.stats ? state.stats.daily_trend : [];
            var c = document.getElementById('trendChart');
            if (!trend || !trend.length) { c.innerHTML = '<div class="table-empty">No trend data</div>'; return; }
            var maxKg = Math.max.apply(null, trend.map(function(d) { return parseFloat(d.total_kg); }));
            if (maxKg === 0) maxKg = 1;
            var todayStr = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
            var html = '<div class="trend-chart">';
            trend.forEach(function(d) {
                var kg = parseFloat(d.total_kg);
                var h = (kg / maxKg * 100).toFixed(1);
                var ds = d.date.slice(0, 10);
                html += '<div class="trend-bar-wrapper"><div class="trend-bar-value">' + formatNum(kg) + '</div><div class="trend-bar' + (ds === todayStr ? ' today' : '') + '" style="height:' + h + '%"></div><div class="trend-bar-date">' + fmtShortDate(ds) + '</div></div>';
            });
            html += '</div>';
            c.innerHTML = html;
        }

        function renderCollections() {
            var tbody = document.getElementById('collectionsBody');
            var txns = state.collections;
            if (!txns || !txns.length) { tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="table-empty">No transactions found</td></tr>'; updateTableInfo(); return; }
            var html = '';
            txns.forEach(function(t) {
                var time = fmtTime(t.transaction_date || t.created_at);
                var name = (t.collector_first_name || '') + (t.collector_last_name ? ' ' + t.collector_last_name : '');
                name = name.trim() || 'Unknown';
                var rText = t.collector_rating ? '⭐ ' + parseFloat(t.collector_rating).toFixed(1) : '—';

                // Payment column
                var payHtml = '';
                var payStatus = t.payment_status || 'unpaid';
                var hasPrice = parseFloat(t.total_price) > 0;
                if (payStatus === 'paid') {
                    payHtml = '<span class="btn-pay paid">✓ Paid</span>';
                } else if (payStatus === 'pending') {
                    payHtml = '<span class="btn-pay pending">⏳ Pending</span>';
                } else if (!hasPrice) {
                    payHtml = '<span class="btn-pay no-price">No price</span>';
                } else {
                    payHtml = '<button class="btn-pay unpaid" onclick="openPayModal(' + t.id + ',' + t.collector_id + ',\'' + esc(name) + '\',' + (parseFloat(t.total_price)||0).toFixed(2) + ',\'' + esc(t.collector_phone || '') + '\',\'' + esc(t.material_type) + '\',' + (parseFloat(t.net_weight_kg)||0).toFixed(1) + ')">Pay GHS ' + (parseFloat(t.total_price)||0).toFixed(2) + '</button>';
                }

                html += '<tr><td class="td-time">' + time + '</td><td>' + esc(name) + '</td><td><span class="material-badge ' + esc(t.material_type) + '">' + esc(t.material_type) + '</span></td><td class="td-weight">' + formatNum(t.net_weight_kg) + '</td><td>' + rText + '</td><td>' + payHtml + '</td></tr>';
            });
            tbody.innerHTML = html;
            updateTableInfo();
        }

        function updateTableInfo() {
            var info = document.getElementById('tableInfo');
            var s = state.collectionsOffset + 1;
            var e = Math.min(state.collectionsOffset + state.collectionsLimit, state.collectionsTotal);
            info.textContent = state.collectionsTotal === 0 ? 'No results' : 'Showing ' + s + '-' + e + ' of ' + state.collectionsTotal;
            document.getElementById('btnPrev').disabled = state.collectionsOffset === 0;
            document.getElementById('btnNext').disabled = (state.collectionsOffset + state.collectionsLimit) >= state.collectionsTotal;
        }

        // ---- SORTING ----
        function sortLocal() {
            var field = state.sortField; var dir = state.sortDir === 'asc' ? 1 : -1;
            state.collections.sort(function(a, b) {
                var va = a[field]; var vb = b[field];
                if (field === 'net_weight_kg') { va = parseFloat(va) || 0; vb = parseFloat(vb) || 0; }
                else if (field === 'transaction_date') { va = new Date(va || a.created_at).getTime(); vb = new Date(vb || b.created_at).getTime(); }
                else if (field === 'collector_name') { va = ((a.collector_first_name || '') + ' ' + (a.collector_last_name || '')).toLowerCase(); vb = ((b.collector_first_name || '') + ' ' + (b.collector_last_name || '')).toLowerCase(); }
                else { va = (va || '').toString().toLowerCase(); vb = (vb || '').toString().toLowerCase(); }
                return va < vb ? -1 * dir : va > vb ? 1 * dir : 0;
            });
        }

        // ---- UTILS ----
        function esc(s) { if (!s) return ''; var d = document.createElement('div'); d.textContent = s; return d.innerHTML; }
        function fmtTime(iso) {
            if (!iso) return '--'; var d = new Date(iso); var diff = Date.now() - d;
            if (diff < 60000) return 'Just now'; if (diff < 3600000) return Math.floor(diff/60000) + 'm ago';
            if (diff < 86400000) return Math.floor(diff/3600000) + 'h ago';
            return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric' }) + ' ' + d.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', hour12: false });
        }
        function fmtShortDate(s) {
            var p = s.split('-'); var d = new Date(+p[0], +p[1]-1, +p[2]);
            return ['Sun','Mon','Tue','Wed','Thu','Fri','Sat'][d.getDay()] + ' ' + ['Jan','Feb','Mar','Apr','May','Jun','Jul','Aug','Sep','Oct','Nov','Dec'][d.getMonth()] + ' ' + d.getDate();
        }

        // ---- EVENTS ----
        window.sortTable = function(field) {
            document.querySelectorAll('thead th').forEach(function(th) { th.classList.remove('sorted-asc', 'sorted-desc'); });
            if (state.sortField === field) state.sortDir = state.sortDir === 'asc' ? 'desc' : 'asc';
            else { state.sortField = field; state.sortDir = field === 'transaction_date' ? 'desc' : 'asc'; }
            var h = document.querySelector('thead th[data-sort="' + field + '"]');
            if (h) h.classList.add(state.sortDir === 'asc' ? 'sorted-asc' : 'sorted-desc');
            sortLocal(); renderCollections();
        };
        window.onFilterChange = function() { state.materialFilter = document.getElementById('materialFilter').value; state.collectionsOffset = 0; loadCollections(); };
        window.prevPage = function() { if (state.collectionsOffset > 0) { state.collectionsOffset = Math.max(0, state.collectionsOffset - state.collectionsLimit); loadCollections(); } };
        window.nextPage = function() { if ((state.collectionsOffset + state.collectionsLimit) < state.collectionsTotal) { state.collectionsOffset += state.collectionsLimit; loadCollections(); } };
        window.refreshAll = function() {
            var btn = document.getElementById('refreshBtn'); btn.textContent = 'Refreshing...'; btn.disabled = true;
            Promise.all([loadStats(), loadCollections()]).then(function() { btn.textContent = 'Refresh'; btn.disabled = false; resetRefreshTimer(); }).catch(function() { btn.textContent = 'Refresh'; btn.disabled = false; });
        };

        // ---- PAYMENT MODAL ----
        var paymentState = { txId: null, collectorId: null, amount: 0, provider: null };

        window.openPayModal = function(txId, collectorId, name, amount, phone, material, weight) {
            paymentState.txId = txId;
            paymentState.collectorId = collectorId;
            paymentState.amount = amount;
            paymentState.provider = null;

            document.getElementById('paySummary').innerHTML =
                '<div class="pay-summary-row"><span class="pay-summary-label">Collector</span><span class="pay-summary-value">' + esc(name) + '</span></div>' +
                '<div class="pay-summary-row"><span class="pay-summary-label">Material</span><span class="pay-summary-value">' + esc(material) + ' — ' + weight + ' kg</span></div>' +
                '<div class="pay-summary-row"><span class="pay-summary-label">Amount</span><span class="pay-summary-value" style="color:#16a34a;font-size:18px;">GHS ' + amount + '</span></div>';

            document.getElementById('payPhone').value = phone || '';
            document.querySelectorAll('.provider-chip').forEach(function(c) { c.classList.remove('selected'); });
            document.getElementById('payConfirmBtn').disabled = true;
            document.getElementById('payOverlay').classList.add('active');
        };

        window.selectProvider = function(provider, chip) {
            paymentState.provider = provider;
            document.querySelectorAll('.provider-chip').forEach(function(c) { c.classList.remove('selected'); });
            chip.classList.add('selected');
            document.getElementById('payConfirmBtn').disabled = false;
        };

        window.closePayModal = function() {
            document.getElementById('payOverlay').classList.remove('active');
        };

        window.confirmPayment = function() {
            var phone = document.getElementById('payPhone').value.trim();
            if (!phone) { alert('Please enter the collector\'s phone number'); return; }
            if (!paymentState.provider) { alert('Please select a payment provider'); return; }

            var btn = document.getElementById('payConfirmBtn');
            btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = 'Processing...';

            fetch('/api/payments/initiate', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    transaction_id: paymentState.txId,
                    operator_id: state.operator ? state.operator.id : null,
                    phone: phone,
                    provider: paymentState.provider
                })
            })
            .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
            .then(function(data) {
                if (data.success) {
                    closePayModal();
                    loadCollections(); // Refresh to show updated payment status
                } else {
                    alert(data.message || 'Payment failed');
                }
            })
            .catch(function() { alert('Connection error'); })
            .finally(function() { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'Send Payment'; });
        };

        // ---- AUTO REFRESH ----
        function resetRefreshTimer() {
            if (state.refreshTimer) clearInterval(state.refreshTimer);
            var countdown = state.refreshInterval / 1000;
            var txt = document.getElementById('refreshText'); var dot = document.getElementById('refreshDot');
            dot.classList.remove('paused'); txt.textContent = 'Auto-refresh: ' + countdown + 's';
            state.refreshTimer = setInterval(function() {
                countdown--;
                if (countdown <= 0) {
                    txt.textContent = 'Refreshing...'; dot.classList.add('paused');
                    Promise.all([loadStats(), loadCollections()]).then(function() { countdown = state.refreshInterval / 1000; dot.classList.remove('paused'); }).catch(function() { countdown = state.refreshInterval / 1000; dot.classList.remove('paused'); });
                } else { txt.textContent = 'Auto-refresh: ' + countdown + 's'; }
            }, 1000);
        }

        // ---- INIT ----
        if (document.readyState === 'loading') document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', checkAuth);
        else checkAuth();
    })();
    </script>

    <!-- Polsia Analytics -->
    <script>
    (function() {
        var slug = 'circul'; if (!slug) return;
        var vid = localStorage.getItem('polsia_vid');
        if (!vid) { vid = 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function(c) { var r = Math.random()*16|0; return (c==='x'?r:(r&0x3|0x8)).toString(16); }); localStorage.setItem('polsia_vid', vid); }
        new Image().src = 'https://polsia.com/api/beacon/pixel?s=' + encodeURIComponent(slug) + '&v=' + encodeURIComponent(vid);
    })();
    </script>
</body>
</html>


===== FILE: public/collect.html =====

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0, maximum-scale=1.0, user-scalable=no">
    <meta name="apple-mobile-web-app-capable" content="yes">
    <meta name="apple-mobile-web-app-status-bar-style" content="black-translucent">
    <meta name="theme-color" content="#0a2e1a">
    <title>Circul - Log Collection</title>
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Space+Grotesk:wght@400;500;600;700&family=DM+Sans:wght@400;500;600&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
    <style>
        *, *::before, *::after { margin: 0; padding: 0; box-sizing: border-box; }

        :root {
            --green-deep: #0a2e1a;
            --green-primary: #16a34a;
            --green-light: #bbf7d0;
            --green-wash: #f0fdf4;
            --amber: #f59e0b;
            --amber-light: #fef3c7;
            --slate: #334155;
            --slate-light: #94a3b8;
            --slate-muted: #64748b;
            --white: #ffffff;
            --off-white: #fafaf9;
            --border: #e2e8f0;
            --red: #ef4444;
            --red-wash: #fef2f2;
            --blue: #3b82f6;
            --blue-wash: #eff6ff;
            --safe-top: env(safe-area-inset-top, 0px);
            --safe-bottom: env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0px);
        }

        html { height: 100%; -webkit-text-size-adjust: 100%; }

        body {
            font-family: 'DM Sans', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, sans-serif;
            color: var(--slate);
            background: var(--off-white);
            min-height: 100%;
            -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased;
            overscroll-behavior: none;
        }

        h1, h2, h3, h4, h5 { font-family: 'Space Grotesk', sans-serif; }

        .app { max-width: 480px; margin: 0 auto; min-height: 100vh; background: var(--white); position: relative; }

        .screen { display: none; opacity: 0; transform: translateY(8px); transition: opacity 0.3s ease, transform 0.3s ease; padding: 0 20px; padding-bottom: calc(24px + var(--safe-bottom)); }
        .screen.active { display: block; }
        .screen.visible { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }

        .header { background: var(--green-deep); padding: calc(16px + var(--safe-top)) 20px 16px; position: sticky; top: 0; z-index: 100; }
        .header-brand { display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 10px; }
        .header-logo { width: 32px; height: 32px; background: var(--green-primary); border-radius: 8px; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; font-family: 'Space Grotesk', sans-serif; font-weight: 700; font-size: 16px; color: var(--white); }
        .header-title { font-family: 'Space Grotesk', sans-serif; font-size: 18px; font-weight: 600; color: var(--white); }
        .header-subtitle { font-size: 12px; color: var(--slate-light); margin-top: 1px; }

        /* AUTH */
        .auth-hero { text-align: center; padding: 48px 20px 32px; }
        .auth-icon { width: 72px; height: 72px; background: var(--green-wash); border-radius: 20px; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; margin: 0 auto 20px; }
        .auth-icon svg { width: 36px; height: 36px; stroke: var(--green-primary); fill: none; stroke-width: 2; stroke-linecap: round; stroke-linejoin: round; }
        .auth-hero h1 { font-size: 24px; font-weight: 700; color: var(--green-deep); margin-bottom: 8px; }
        .auth-hero p { font-size: 15px; color: var(--slate-muted); line-height: 1.5; }

    <script>
    (function() {
        'use strict';

        var state = {
            collector: null,
            selectedMaterial: null,
            selectedRating: 0,
            lastTransactionId: null,
            gpsLat: null,
            gpsLng: null,
            gpsStatus: 'idle',
            isSubmitting: false,
            gpsWatchId: null
        };

        // ---- INIT ----
        function init() {
            var saved = localStorage.getItem('circul_collector');
            if (saved) {
                try {
                    state.collector = JSON.parse(saved);
                    showScreen('collect');
                    loadCollectorData();
                } catch (e) {
                    localStorage.removeItem('circul_collector');
                    showScreen('auth');
                }
            } else {
                showScreen('auth');
            }
            updateTimeOfDay();
        }

        function updateTimeOfDay() {
            var hour = new Date().getHours();
            var el = document.getElementById('time-of-day');
            if (el) {
                if (hour < 12) el.textContent = 'morning';
                else if (hour < 17) el.textContent = 'afternoon';
                else el.textContent = 'evening';
            }
        }

        // ---- SCREENS ----
        function showScreen(name) {
            var screens = document.querySelectorAll('.screen');
            for (var i = 0; i < screens.length; i++) screens[i].classList.remove('active', 'visible');
            var target = document.getElementById(name + '-screen');
            if (target) {
                target.classList.add('active');
                requestAnimationFrame(function() { requestAnimationFrame(function() { target.classList.add('visible'); }); });
            }
            if (name === 'collect') {
                if (state.collector) {
                    var fullName = state.collector.first_name;
                    if (state.collector.last_name) fullName += ' ' + state.collector.last_name;
                    document.getElementById('collector-name').textContent = fullName;
                }
                startGPS();
            } else {
                stopGPS();
            }
        }

        // ---- TABS ----
        window.switchTab = function(tabName) {
            var tabs = document.querySelectorAll('.tab');
            for (var i = 0; i < tabs.length; i++) tabs[i].classList.toggle('active', tabs[i].getAttribute('data-tab') === tabName);
            var panels = document.querySelectorAll('.form-panel');
            for (var j = 0; j < panels.length; j++) panels[j].classList.remove('active');
            document.getElementById(tabName + '-panel').classList.add('active');
            hideError('login'); hideError('register');
        };

        // ---- AUTH ----
        window.handleLogin = function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var phone = document.getElementById('login-phone').value.trim();
            var pin = document.getElementById('login-pin').value.trim();
            if (!phone || !pin) { showError('login', 'Please enter your phone number and PIN.'); return; }
            setButtonLoading('login-btn', true); hideError('login');
            apiPost('/api/collectors/login', { phone: phone, pin: pin })
                .then(function(data) {
                    if (data.success) { state.collector = data.collector; localStorage.setItem('circul_collector', JSON.stringify(data.collector)); showScreen('collect'); loadCollectorData(); }
                    else showError('login', data.message || 'Invalid phone or PIN.');
                })
                .catch(function(err) { showError('login', err.message || 'Connection error.'); })
                .finally(function() { setButtonLoading('login-btn', false); });
        };

        window.handleRegister = function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var first_name = document.getElementById('reg-first-name').value.trim();
            var last_name = document.getElementById('reg-last-name').value.trim();
            var phone = document.getElementById('reg-phone').value.trim();
            var pin = document.getElementById('reg-pin').value.trim();
            var region = document.getElementById('reg-region').value.trim();
            if (!first_name || !phone || !pin) { showError('register', 'First name, phone, and PIN are required.'); return; }
            if (pin.length < 4 || pin.length > 6) { showError('register', 'PIN must be 4-6 digits.'); return; }
            if (!/^\d+$/.test(pin)) { showError('register', 'PIN must be numbers only.'); return; }
            setButtonLoading('register-btn', true); hideError('register');
            apiPost('/api/collectors', { first_name: first_name, last_name: last_name, phone: phone, pin: pin, region: region || undefined })
                .then(function(data) {
                    if (data.success) { state.collector = data.collector; localStorage.setItem('circul_collector', JSON.stringify(data.collector)); showScreen('collect'); loadCollectorData(); showToast('Account created! Welcome to Circul.'); }
                    else showError('register', data.message || 'Registration failed.');
                })
                .catch(function(err) { showError('register', err.message || 'Connection error.'); })
                .finally(function() { setButtonLoading('register-btn', false); });
        };

        window.handleLogout = function() {
            state.collector = null; state.selectedMaterial = null; state.gpsLat = null; state.gpsLng = null;
            localStorage.removeItem('circul_collector'); stopGPS(); resetCollectionForm(); showScreen('auth');
        };

        // ---- MATERIAL ----
        window.selectMaterial = function(btn) {
            var all = document.querySelectorAll('.material-btn');
            for (var i = 0; i < all.length; i++) all[i].classList.remove('selected');
            btn.classList.add('selected');
            state.selectedMaterial = btn.getAttribute('data-material');
        };

        window.updateNetWeight = function() {
            var gross = parseFloat(document.getElementById('weight-input').value) || 0;
            var price = parseFloat(document.getElementById('price-input').value) || 0;
            var total = gross * price;
            document.getElementById('total-price-display').value = total > 0 ? total.toFixed(2) : '';
        };

        // ---- GPS ----
        function startGPS() {
            if (!navigator.geolocation) { setGPSStatus('failed', 'GPS not available'); return; }
            setGPSStatus('acquiring', 'Acquiring GPS...');
            state.gpsWatchId = navigator.geolocation.watchPosition(
                function(pos) {
                    state.gpsLat = pos.coords.latitude; state.gpsLng = pos.coords.longitude;
                    setGPSStatus('locked', 'GPS locked (' + Math.round(pos.coords.accuracy) + 'm)');
                    document.getElementById('gps-coords').textContent = state.gpsLat.toFixed(5) + ', ' + state.gpsLng.toFixed(5);
                },
                function(err) {
                    var msg = err.code === 1 ? 'Location denied' : err.code === 2 ? 'GPS signal lost' : 'GPS timed out';
                    setGPSStatus('failed', msg);
                },
                { enableHighAccuracy: true, timeout: 15000, maximumAge: 30000 }
            );
        }

        function stopGPS() {
            if (state.gpsWatchId !== null) { navigator.geolocation.clearWatch(state.gpsWatchId); state.gpsWatchId = null; }
        }

        function setGPSStatus(status, text) {
            state.gpsStatus = status;
            var dot = document.getElementById('gps-dot');
            dot.className = 'gps-dot';
            if (status === 'acquiring') dot.classList.add('acquiring');
            else if (status === 'locked') dot.classList.add('locked');
            else if (status === 'failed') dot.classList.add('failed');
            document.getElementById('gps-text').textContent = text;
            if (status !== 'locked') document.getElementById('gps-coords').textContent = '';
        }

        // ---- SUBMIT ----
        window.handleSubmitCollection = function() {
            if (state.isSubmitting) return;

            var weight = parseFloat(document.getElementById('weight-input').value);
            var notes = document.getElementById('notes-input').value.trim();
            var pricePerKg = parseFloat(document.getElementById('price-input').value) || null;
            var buyerName = document.getElementById('buyer-input').value.trim();

            if (!state.selectedMaterial) { showError('collect', 'Please select a material type.'); return; }
            if (!weight || weight <= 0) { showError('collect', 'Please enter a valid weight.'); return; }
            if (weight > 5000) { showError('collect', 'Weight seems too high.'); return; }

            hideError('collect');
            state.isSubmitting = true;
            setButtonLoading('submit-btn', true);

            var payload = {
                collector_id: state.collector.id,
                material_type: state.selectedMaterial,
                gross_weight_kg: weight,
                price_per_kg: pricePerKg,
                lat: state.gpsLat,
                lng: state.gpsLng,
                notes: notes || (buyerName ? 'Buyer: ' + buyerName : undefined)
            };

            apiPost('/api/transactions', payload)
                .then(function(data) {
                    if (data.success) {
                        var net = parseFloat(data.transaction.net_weight_kg) || weight;
                        showToast(net.toFixed(1) + ' kg ' + state.selectedMaterial + ' logged!');
                        state.lastTransactionId = data.transaction.id;
                        resetCollectionForm();
                        loadCollectorData();
                        // Show rating modal
                        showRatingModal();
                    } else {
                        showError('collect', data.message || 'Failed to log transaction.');
                    }
                })
                .catch(function(err) { showError('collect', err.message || 'Connection error.'); })
                .finally(function() { state.isSubmitting = false; setButtonLoading('submit-btn', false); });
        };

        function resetCollectionForm() {
            state.selectedMaterial = null;
            var btns = document.querySelectorAll('.material-btn');
            for (var i = 0; i < btns.length; i++) btns[i].classList.remove('selected');
            document.getElementById('weight-input').value = '';
            document.getElementById('price-input').value = '';
            document.getElementById('buyer-input').value = '';
            document.getElementById('notes-input').value = '';
            document.getElementById('total-price-display').value = '';
            hideError('collect');
        }

        // ---- RATING ----
        function showRatingModal() {
            state.selectedRating = 0;
            var stars = document.querySelectorAll('.star');
            for (var i = 0; i < stars.length; i++) stars[i].classList.remove('active');
            document.getElementById('submit-rating-btn').disabled = true;
            document.getElementById('rating-overlay').classList.add('active');
        }

        window.selectRating = function(rating) {
            state.selectedRating = rating;
            var stars = document.querySelectorAll('.star');
            for (var i = 0; i < stars.length; i++) {
                stars[i].classList.toggle('active', parseInt(stars[i].getAttribute('data-rating')) <= rating);
            }
            document.getElementById('submit-rating-btn').disabled = false;
        };

        window.submitRating = function() {
            if (!state.selectedRating || !state.collector) return;
            setButtonLoading('submit-rating-btn', true);

            apiPost('/api/ratings', {
                transaction_id: state.lastTransactionId,
                collector_id: state.collector.id,
                rating: state.selectedRating
            })
            .then(function(data) {
                if (data.success) showToast('Rating submitted!');
            })
            .catch(function() { /* silent fail for ratings */ })
            .finally(function() {
                setButtonLoading('submit-rating-btn', false);
                document.getElementById('rating-overlay').classList.remove('active');
            });
        };

        window.skipRating = function() {
            document.getElementById('rating-overlay').classList.remove('active');
        };

        // ---- LOAD DATA ----
        function loadCollectorData() {
            if (!state.collector) return;
            apiGet('/api/collectors/' + state.collector.id + '/stats')
                .then(function(data) {
                    if (data.success) {
                        document.getElementById('today-weight').textContent = formatWeight(parseFloat(data.stats.today.today_kg) || 0);
                        document.getElementById('today-count').textContent = parseInt(data.stats.today.today_count) || 0;
                        renderRecentTransactions(data.stats.recent_transactions || []);
                    }
                }).catch(function() {});
        }

        function renderRecentTransactions(transactions) {
            var container = document.getElementById('recent-list');
            if (!transactions || transactions.length === 0) {
                container.innerHTML = '<div class="recent-empty">No transactions yet. Log your first one above.</div>';
                return;
            }
            var items = transactions.slice(0, 5);
            var html = '';
            for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                var t = items[i];
                var weight = parseFloat(t.net_weight_kg) || 0;
                var price = t.total_price ? ' | GHS ' + parseFloat(t.total_price).toFixed(2) : '';
                html += '<div class="recent-item">' +
                    '<div class="recent-badge">' + escapeHtml(t.material_type) + '</div>' +
                    '<div class="recent-info">' +
                        '<div class="recent-material">' + escapeHtml(t.material_type) + price + '</div>' +
                        '<div class="recent-meta">' + formatTimeAgo(t.transaction_date || t.created_at) + '</div>' +
                    '</div>' +
                    '<div class="recent-weight">' + formatWeight(weight) + ' kg</div>' +
                '</div>';
            }
            container.innerHTML = html;
        }

        // ---- API ----
        function apiPost(url, body) {
            return fetch(url, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify(body) })
                .then(function(res) { return res.json().then(function(data) { if (!res.ok && !data.message) throw new Error('Request failed'); return data; }); });
        }
        function apiGet(url) { return fetch(url).then(function(res) { return res.json(); }); }

        // ---- UI HELPERS ----
        function showError(prefix, message) { var el = document.getElementById(prefix + '-error'); if (el) { el.textContent = message; el.classList.add('visible'); } }
        function hideError(prefix) { var el = document.getElementById(prefix + '-error'); if (el) el.classList.remove('visible'); }

        function setButtonLoading(btnId, loading) {
            var btn = document.getElementById(btnId); if (!btn) return;
            var textEl = btn.querySelector('.btn-text');
            if (loading) { btn.disabled = true; if (textEl) textEl.style.display = 'none'; var s = document.createElement('div'); s.className = 'spinner'; s.id = btnId + '-spinner'; btn.appendChild(s); }
            else { btn.disabled = false; if (textEl) textEl.style.display = ''; var es = document.getElementById(btnId + '-spinner'); if (es) es.remove(); }
        }

        var toastTimer = null;
        function showToast(message, isError) {
            var toast = document.getElementById('toast'); var textEl = document.getElementById('toast-text');
            textEl.textContent = message; toast.classList.toggle('error', !!isError);
            var iconSvg = toast.querySelector('.toast-icon');
            iconSvg.innerHTML = isError ? '<line x1="18" y1="6" x2="6" y2="18"/><line x1="6" y1="6" x2="18" y2="18"/>' : '<polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12"/>';
            toast.classList.add('show');
            if (toastTimer) clearTimeout(toastTimer);
            toastTimer = setTimeout(function() { toast.classList.remove('show'); }, 3000);
        }

        function formatWeight(kg) { if (kg >= 1000) return (kg/1000).toFixed(1) + 'k'; if (kg === Math.floor(kg)) return kg.toString(); return kg.toFixed(1); }

        function formatTimeAgo(dateStr) {
            if (!dateStr) return '';
            var d = new Date(dateStr); var now = new Date(); var diff = now - d; var mins = Math.floor(diff / 60000);
            if (mins < 1) return 'Just now'; if (mins < 60) return mins + ' min ago';
            var hrs = Math.floor(mins / 60); if (hrs < 24) return hrs + 'h ago';
            var days = Math.floor(hrs / 24); if (days === 1) return 'Yesterday'; if (days < 7) return days + 'd ago';
            return d.toLocaleDateString('en-GB', { day: 'numeric', month: 'short' });
        }

        function escapeHtml(str) { if (!str) return ''; var d = document.createElement('div'); d.textContent = str; return d.innerHTML; }

        // ---- RIPPLE ----
        document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            var btn = e.target.closest('.btn-primary, .btn-secondary');
            if (!btn) return;
            var rect = btn.getBoundingClientRect(); var size = Math.max(rect.width, rect.height) * 2;
            var ripple = document.createElement('span'); ripple.className = 'ripple';
            ripple.style.width = size + 'px'; ripple.style.height = size + 'px';
            ripple.style.left = (e.clientX - rect.left - size/2) + 'px'; ripple.style.top = (e.clientY - rect.top - size/2) + 'px';
            btn.appendChild(ripple); setTimeout(function() { ripple.remove(); }, 500);
        });

        // ---- BOOT ----
        if (document.readyState === 'loading') document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
        else init();
    })();
    </script>

    <!-- Polsia Analytics -->
    <script>
    (function() {
        var slug = 'circul'; if (!slug) return;
        var vid = localStorage.getItem('polsia_vid');
        if (!vid) { vid = 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function(c) { var r = Math.random()*16|0; return (c==='x'?r:(r&0x3|0x8)).toString(16); }); localStorage.setItem('polsia_vid', vid); }
        new Image().src = 'https://polsia.com/api/beacon/pixel?s=' + encodeURIComponent(slug) + '&v=' + encodeURIComponent(vid);
    })();
    </script>
</body>
</html>


===== FILE: public/admin.html =====

  <div class="login-card">

    </div>

      <label>Email</label>
      <input type="email" id="login-email" placeholder="hello@repatrn.com" autocomplete="email">
    </div>
    <div class="form-group">
      <label>Password</label>
      <input type="password" id="login-password" placeholder="••••••••" autocomplete="current-password">
    </div>
    <button class="btn" onclick="adminLogin()">Sign In</button>
    <div id="login-error" class="error-msg"></div>
  </div>

<!-- MAIN SCREEN -->
<div id="main-screen">
  <div class="topbar">
    <div class="brand">Circul <span>Admin</span></div>
    <div class="user-info">
      <span id="admin-email-display"></span>
      <button onclick="logout()">Logout</button>
    </div>
  </div>
  <div class="content">
    <div class="tabs">
      <button class="tab active" onclick="showTab('overview', this)">Overview</button>
      <button class="tab" onclick="showTab('collectors', this)">Collectors</button>
      <button class="tab" onclick="showTab('transactions', this)">Transactions</button>
      <button class="tab" onclick="showTab('operators', this)">Operators</button>
      <button class="tab" onclick="showTab('buyers', this)">Buyers</button>
      <button class="tab" onclick="showTab('reputation', this)">Reputation</button>
    </div>

    <!-- OVERVIEW -->
    <div id="tab-overview">
      <div class="stat-grid" id="stat-grid"><div class="loading">Loading stats…</div></div>
      <div class="mat-grid" id="mat-grid"></div>
      <div class="panel" id="system-health-panel">
        <h3 style="margin-bottom:16px;font-size:1rem">System Health</h3>
        <div id="system-health-content" class="loading">Loading…</div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- COLLECTORS -->
    <div id="tab-collectors" style="display:none">
      <div class="section-header"><h3>All Collectors</h3></div>
      <table>
        <thead><tr><th>Name</th><th>Phone</th><th>Region</th><th>Rating</th><th>Total kg</th><th>Transactions</th><th>Joined</th></tr></thead>
        <tbody id="collectors-tbody"><tr><td colspan="7" class="loading">Loading…</td></tr></tbody>
      </table>
    </div>

    <!-- TRANSACTIONS -->
    <div id="tab-transactions" style="display:none">
      <div class="section-header"><h3>All Transactions</h3></div>
      <table>
        <thead><tr><th>Date</th><th>Collector</th><th>Material</th><th>Gross kg</th><th>Net kg</th><th>Price/kg</th><th>Total</th><th>Payment</th><th>Operator</th></tr></thead>
        <tbody id="transactions-tbody"><tr><td colspan="9" class="loading">Loading…</td></tr></tbody>

    <!-- OPERATORS -->
    <div id="tab-operators" style="display:none">

          <select id="role-filter" onchange="loadOperators()" style="padding:6px 10px;border:1.5px solid var(--border);border-radius:7px;font-family:inherit;font-size:0.85rem">
            <option value="">All Roles</option>
            <option value="collector">Collector</option>
            <option value="aggregator">Aggregator</option>

      <table>
        <thead><tr><th>Name</th><th>Company</th><th>Email</th><th>Role</th><th>Prices Set</th><th>Status</th><th>Actions</th></tr></thead>
        <tbody id="buyers-tbody"><tr><td colspan="7" class="loading">Loading…</td></tr></tbody>
      </table>
    </div>

    <!-- REPUTATION -->
    <div id="tab-reputation" style="display:none">
      <div class="section-header"><h3>Operator Reputation</h3></div>
      <table>
        <thead><tr><th>Name</th><th>Role</th><th>City</th><th>Avg Rating</th><th>Rating Count</th><th>Actions</th></tr></thead>
        <tbody id="reputation-tbody"><tr><td colspan="6" class="loading">Loading…</td></tr></tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

<script>
let adminToken = localStorage.getItem('circul_admin_token');
let adminData = null;
let currentTab = 'overview';

// Auto-login if token exists
window.onload = () => {
  if (adminToken) {
    showMain();
    loadCurrentTab();
  }
};

// Enter key on login
document.getElementById('login-password').addEventListener('keydown', e => { if (e.key === 'Enter') adminLogin(); });

async function adminLogin() {
  const email = document.getElementById('login-email').value.trim();
  const password = document.getElementById('login-password').value;
  const errEl = document.getElementById('login-error');
  errEl.textContent = '';
  if (!email || !password) { errEl.textContent = 'Email and password required'; return; }
  try {
    const res = await fetch('/api/admin/login', {
      method: 'POST', headers: {'Content-Type':'application/json'},
      body: JSON.stringify({ email, password })
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    if (!data.success) { errEl.textContent = data.message || 'Login failed'; return; }
    adminToken = data.token;
    adminData = data.admin;
    localStorage.setItem('circul_admin_token', adminToken);
    showMain();
    loadCurrentTab();
  } catch (e) {
    errEl.textContent = 'Network error. Try again.';
  }
}

function showMain() {
  document.getElementById('login-screen').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('main-screen').style.display = 'flex';
  const stored = localStorage.getItem('circul_admin_token');
  if (stored && !adminData) {
    // try to decode email from token
    try {
      const b64 = stored.split('.')[0];
      adminData = JSON.parse(atob(b64.replace(/-/g,'+').replace(/_/g,'/')));
    } catch {}
  }
  if (adminData) document.getElementById('admin-email-display').textContent = adminData.email || 'Admin';
}

function logout() {
  localStorage.removeItem('circul_admin_token');
  adminToken = null;
  document.getElementById('main-screen').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('login-screen').style.display = 'flex';
}

function authHeaders() {
  return { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + adminToken };
}

async function apiFetch(url, opts = {}) {
  const res = await fetch(url, { headers: authHeaders(), ...opts });
  if (res.status === 401) { logout(); return null; }
  return res.json();
}

function showTab(tab, el) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
  el.classList.add('active');
  document.querySelectorAll('[id^=tab-]').forEach(t => t.style.display = 'none');
  document.getElementById('tab-' + tab).style.display = '';
  currentTab = tab;
  loadTab(tab);
}

function loadCurrentTab() { loadTab(currentTab); }

function loadTab(tab) {
  if (tab === 'overview') loadOverview();
  else if (tab === 'collectors') loadCollectors();
  else if (tab === 'transactions') loadTransactions();
  else if (tab === 'operators') loadOperators();
  else if (tab === 'buyers') loadBuyers();
  else if (tab === 'reputation') loadReputation();
}

async function loadOverview() {
  const data = await apiFetch('/api/admin/stats');
  if (!data || !data.success) return;
  const s = data.stats;

  // Role breakdown from operators list
  const opsData = await apiFetch('/api/admin/operators');
  const roleCounts = { collector:0, aggregator:0, processor:0, converter:0, operator:0, admin:0 };
  if (opsData && opsData.operators) {
    opsData.operators.forEach(o => { if (roleCounts[o.role] !== undefined) roleCounts[o.role]++; });
  }

  document.getElementById('stat-grid').innerHTML = `
    <div class="stat-card"><div class="num">${s.collectors}</div><div class="label">Collectors (USSD)</div></div>
    <div class="stat-card"><div class="num">${roleCounts.aggregator}</div><div class="label">Aggregators</div></div>
    <div class="stat-card"><div class="num">${roleCounts.processor}</div><div class="label">Processors</div></div>
    <div class="stat-card"><div class="num">${roleCounts.converter}</div><div class="label">Converters</div></div>
    <div class="stat-card"><div class="num">${s.transactions}</div><div class="label">Transactions</div></div>
    <div class="stat-card"><div class="num">${parseFloat(s.total_volume_kg).toFixed(1)}</div><div class="label">Total kg collected</div></div>
  `;
  const materials = ['PET','HDPE','LDPE','PP'];
  const matMap = {};
  (s.by_material || []).forEach(m => matMap[m.material_type] = m);
  document.getElementById('mat-grid').innerHTML = materials.map(m => {
    const d = matMap[m] || {};
    return `<div class="mat-card">
      <div class="mat-name">${m}</div>
      <div class="mat-kg">${parseFloat(d.total_kg || 0).toFixed(1)} kg</div>
      <div class="mat-txns">${d.count || 0} transactions</div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');

  // System health
  const txnData = await apiFetch('/api/admin/transactions?limit=1');
  const paySuccess = s.transactions > 0 ? 'N/A' : '—';
  document.getElementById('system-health-content').innerHTML = `
    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(3,1fr);gap:16px">
      <div><div style="font-size:1.5rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--green-dark)">${s.transactions}</div><div style="font-size:0.82rem;color:var(--slate-light)">Total DB transactions</div></div>
      <div><div style="font-size:1.5rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--green-dark)">${s.operators}</div><div style="font-size:0.82rem;color:var(--slate-light)">Active operators (all roles)</div></div>
      <div><div style="font-size:1.5rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--green-dark)">${s.buyers}</div><div style="font-size:0.82rem;color:var(--slate-light)">Legacy buyer accounts</div></div>
    </div>
  `;
}

async function loadCollectors() {
  const data = await apiFetch('/api/admin/collectors');
  if (!data || !data.success) return;
  const tbody = document.getElementById('collectors-tbody');
  if (!data.collectors.length) { tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="7" class="empty">No collectors yet.</td></tr>'; return; }
  tbody.innerHTML = data.collectors.map(c => `
    <tr>
      <td>${escHtml(c.first_name + ' ' + c.last_name)}</td>
      <td>${escHtml(c.phone || '—')}</td>
      <td>${escHtml(c.region || '—')}</td>
      <td>${c.average_rating ? '⭐ ' + parseFloat(c.average_rating).toFixed(1) : '—'}</td>
      <td>${parseFloat(c.total_weight_kg).toFixed(2)} kg</td>
      <td>${c.transaction_count}</td>
      <td>${fmtDate(c.created_at)}</td>
    </tr>`).join('');
}

async function loadTransactions() {
  const data = await apiFetch('/api/admin/transactions?limit=200');
  if (!data || !data.success) return;
  const tbody = document.getElementById('transactions-tbody');
  if (!data.transactions.length) { tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="9" class="empty">No transactions yet.</td></tr>'; return; }
  tbody.innerHTML = data.transactions.map(t => `
    <tr>
      <td>${fmtDate(t.transaction_date)}</td>
      <td>${escHtml(t.collector_name || '—')}</td>
      <td><span class="badge badge-green">${t.material_type}</span></td>
      <td>${parseFloat(t.gross_weight_kg).toFixed(2)}</td>
      <td>${parseFloat(t.net_weight_kg).toFixed(2)}</td>
      <td>${t.price_per_kg ? 'GHS ' + parseFloat(t.price_per_kg).toFixed(2) : '—'}</td>
      <td>${t.total_price ? 'GHS ' + parseFloat(t.total_price).toFixed(2) : '—'}</td>
      <td><span class="badge ${t.payment_status === 'paid' ? 'badge-green' : t.payment_status === 'pending' ? 'badge-amber' : 'badge-gray'}">${t.payment_status || 'unpaid'}</span></td>
      <td>${escHtml(t.operator_name || '—')}</td>
    </tr>`).join('');
}

const ROLE_BADGE_CLASS = { admin:'badge-blue', aggregator:'badge-green', processor:'badge-blue', converter:'badge-amber', collector:'badge-gray', operator:'badge-gray' };

async function loadOperators() {
  const roleFilter = document.getElementById('role-filter') ? document.getElementById('role-filter').value : '';
  const data = await apiFetch('/api/admin/operators');
  if (!data || !data.success) return;
  const tbody = document.getElementById('operators-tbody');
  let ops = data.operators;
  if (roleFilter) ops = ops.filter(o => o.role === roleFilter);
  if (!ops.length) { tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="8" class="empty">No operators found.</td></tr>'; return; }
  tbody.innerHTML = ops.map(op => `
    <tr>
      <td>${escHtml(op.name)}</td>
      <td>${escHtml(op.company || '—')}</td>
      <td>${escHtml(op.phone || '—')}</td>
      <td><code style="background:#f1f5f9;padding:2px 6px;border-radius:4px">${op.pin || '—'}</code></td>
      <td><span class="badge ${ROLE_BADGE_CLASS[op.role] || 'badge-gray'}">${op.role}</span></td>
      <td>${escHtml(op.city || '—')}</td>
      <td><span class="badge ${op.is_active ? 'badge-green' : 'badge-red'}">${op.is_active ? 'Active' : 'Inactive'}</span></td>
      <td>
        <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="editOperator(${JSON.stringify(op).replace(/"/g,'&quot;')})">Edit</button>
        ${op.is_active ? `<button class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" style="margin-left:6px" onclick="toggleOperator(${op.id},false)">Disable</button>` : `<button class="btn btn-sm" style="margin-left:6px" onclick="toggleOperator(${op.id},true)">Enable</button>`}
      </td>
    </tr>`).join('');
}

async function loadReputation() {
  const data = await apiFetch('/api/admin/operators');
  if (!data || !data.success) return;
  const tbody = document.getElementById('reputation-tbody');
  const ops = data.operators.filter(o => ['aggregator','processor','converter','collector'].includes(o.role));
  if (!ops.length) { tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="empty">No operators with reputation data.</td></tr>'; return; }

  // Fetch ratings for each operator in parallel (cap at 20)
  const slice = ops.slice(0, 20);
  const ratingsData = await Promise.all(slice.map(op =>
    fetch(`/api/ratings/operator/${op.id}`, { headers: authHeaders() }).then(r => r.json()).catch(() => ({ success: false }))
  ));

  tbody.innerHTML = slice.map((op, i) => {
    const rd = ratingsData[i];
    const avg = rd && rd.summary ? rd.summary.avg_rating || '—' : '—';
    const cnt = rd && rd.summary ? rd.summary.count || 0 : 0;
    return `<tr>
      <td>${escHtml(op.name)}</td>
      <td><span class="badge ${ROLE_BADGE_CLASS[op.role] || 'badge-gray'}">${op.role}</span></td>
      <td>${escHtml(op.city || '—')}</td>
      <td>${avg !== '—' ? '⭐ ' + avg : '—'}</td>
      <td>${cnt}</td>
      <td>
        <button class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="flagOperator(${op.id})" title="Flag for review">Flag</button>
      </td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}

async function flagOperator(id) {
  if (!confirm('Flag this operator for review? This will mark them as flagged but keep them active.')) return;
  await apiFetch(`/api/admin/operators/${id}`, { method: 'PUT', body: JSON.stringify({ is_flagged: true }) });
  loadReputation();
}

async function loadBuyers() {
  const data = await apiFetch('/api/admin/buyers');
  if (!data || !data.success) return;
  const tbody = document.getElementById('buyers-tbody');
  if (!data.buyers.length) { tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="7" class="empty">No buyers yet. Add aggregators and processors above.</td></tr>'; return; }
  tbody.innerHTML = data.buyers.map(b => {
    const priceCount = (b.prices || []).length;
    const priceDisplay = priceCount ? `${priceCount}/4 materials` : '—';
    return `
    <tr>
      <td>${escHtml(b.name)}</td>
      <td>${escHtml(b.company || '—')}</td>
      <td>${escHtml(b.email)}</td>
      <td><span class="badge ${b.role === 'aggregator' ? 'badge-green' : 'badge-blue'}">${b.role}</span></td>
      <td>${priceDisplay}</td>
      <td><span class="badge ${b.is_active ? 'badge-green' : 'badge-red'}">${b.is_active ? 'Active' : 'Inactive'}</span></td>
      <td>
        <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="editBuyer(${JSON.stringify(b).replace(/"/g,'&quot;')})">Edit</button>
        ${b.is_active ? `<button class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" style="margin-left:6px" onclick="toggleBuyer(${b.id},false)">Disable</button>` : `<button class="btn btn-sm" style="margin-left:6px" onclick="toggleBuyer(${b.id},true)">Enable</button>`}
      </td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}

// OPERATOR MODAL
function openModal(type) {
  if (type === 'operator') {
    document.getElementById('op-modal-title').textContent = 'Add Operator';
    document.getElementById('op-edit-id').value = '';
    ['op-name','op-company','op-phone','op-pin'].forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).value = '');
    document.getElementById('op-role').value = 'operator';
    document.getElementById('op-error').textContent = '';
  } else {
    document.getElementById('buyer-modal-title').textContent = 'Add Buyer';
    document.getElementById('buyer-edit-id').value = '';
    ['buyer-name','buyer-company','buyer-email','buyer-password'].forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).value = '');
    document.getElementById('buyer-role').value = 'aggregator';
    document.getElementById('buyer-error').textContent = '';
  }
  document.getElementById('modal-' + type).classList.add('open');
}
function closeModal(type) { document.getElementById('modal-' + type).classList.remove('open'); }

function editOperator(op) {
  document.getElementById('op-modal-title').textContent = 'Edit Operator';
  document.getElementById('op-edit-id').value = op.id;
  document.getElementById('op-name').value = op.name || '';
  document.getElementById('op-company').value = op.company || '';
  document.getElementById('op-phone').value = op.phone || '';
  document.getElementById('op-pin').value = op.pin || '';
  document.getElementById('op-role').value = op.role || 'operator';
  document.getElementById('op-error').textContent = '';
  document.getElementById('modal-operator').classList.add('open');
}

function editBuyer(b) {
  document.getElementById('buyer-modal-title').textContent = 'Edit Buyer';
  document.getElementById('buyer-edit-id').value = b.id;
  document.getElementById('buyer-name').value = b.name || '';
  document.getElementById('buyer-company').value = b.company || '';
  document.getElementById('buyer-email').value = b.email || '';
  document.getElementById('buyer-password').value = '';
  document.getElementById('buyer-role').value = b.role || 'aggregator';
  document.getElementById('buyer-error').textContent = '';
  document.getElementById('modal-buyer').classList.add('open');
}

async function saveOperator() {
  const id = document.getElementById('op-edit-id').value;
  const body = {
    name: document.getElementById('op-name').value.trim(),
    company: document.getElementById('op-company').value.trim(),
    phone: document.getElementById('op-phone').value.trim(),
    pin: document.getElementById('op-pin').value.trim(),
    role: document.getElementById('op-role').value
  };
  const errEl = document.getElementById('op-error');
  errEl.textContent = '';
  const url = id ? `/api/admin/operators/${id}` : '/api/admin/operators';
  const method = id ? 'PUT' : 'POST';
  const data = await apiFetch(url, { method, body: JSON.stringify(body) });
  if (!data) return;
  if (!data.success) { errEl.textContent = data.message || 'Error saving'; return; }
  closeModal('operator');
  loadOperators();
}

async function saveBuyer() {
  const id = document.getElementById('buyer-edit-id').value;
  const body = {
    name: document.getElementById('buyer-name').value.trim(),
    company: document.getElementById('buyer-company').value.trim(),
    email: document.getElementById('buyer-email').value.trim(),
    password: document.getElementById('buyer-password').value,
    role: document.getElementById('buyer-role').value
  };
  if (!id && !body.password) { document.getElementById('buyer-error').textContent = 'Password required for new buyers'; return; }
  if (!body.password) delete body.password;
  const errEl = document.getElementById('buyer-error');
  errEl.textContent = '';
  const url = id ? `/api/admin/buyers/${id}` : '/api/admin/buyers';
  const method = id ? 'PUT' : 'POST';
  const data = await apiFetch(url, { method, body: JSON.stringify(body) });
  if (!data) return;
  if (!data.success) { errEl.textContent = data.message || 'Error saving'; return; }
  closeModal('buyer');
  loadBuyers();
}

async function toggleOperator(id, active) {
  await apiFetch(`/api/admin/operators/${id}`, { method: 'PUT', body: JSON.stringify({ is_active: active }) });
  loadOperators();
}

async function toggleBuyer(id, active) {
  await apiFetch(`/api/admin/buyers/${id}`, { method: 'PUT', body: JSON.stringify({ is_active: active }) });
  loadBuyers();
}

// Close modals on overlay click
document.querySelectorAll('.modal-overlay').forEach(overlay => {
  overlay.addEventListener('click', e => { if (e.target === overlay) overlay.classList.remove('open'); });
});

// Helpers
function escHtml(s) { return String(s || '').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;'); }
function fmtDate(d) {
  if (!d) return '—';
  const dt = new Date(d);
  return dt.toLocaleDateString('en-GB', { day:'2-digit', month:'short', year:'numeric' });
}
</script>
</body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Circul - The Waste-to-Resource Operating System</title>
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Space+Grotesk:wght@400;500;600;700&family=DM+Sans:wght@400;500&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
    <style>
        * { margin: 0; padding: 0; box-sizing: border-box; }
        
        :root {
            --green-deep: #0a2e1a;
            --green-primary: #16a34a;
            --green-light: #bbf7d0;
            --green-wash: #f0fdf4;
            --amber: #f59e0b;
            --amber-light: #fef3c7;
            --slate: #334155;
            --slate-light: #94a3b8;
            --white: #ffffff;
            --off-white: #fafaf9;
        }

        body {
            font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
            color: var(--slate);
            background: var(--white);
            overflow-x: hidden;

    <section class="prices-widget" id="prices-section" style="padding:80px 32px;background:var(--off-white);">
        <div style="max-width:1100px;margin:0 auto;">

    <script>
    function loadPriceWidget() {
        var city = document.getElementById('price-city').value;
        var material = document.getElementById('price-material').value;
        var url = '/api/prices?role=collector&city=' + encodeURIComponent(city) + (material ? '&material=' + material : '');
        var container = document.getElementById('price-widget-content');
        container.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:32px;text-align:center;color:#94a3b8;font-size:0.9rem;">Loading…</div>';
        fetch(url).then(function(r) { return r.json(); }).then(function(data) {
            if (!data.success) { container.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:32px;text-align:center;color:#94a3b8;">No price data available yet.</div>'; return; }
            var near = data.near_prices || [];
            var national = data.national_averages || [];
            var html = '';
            if (near.length > 0) {
                html += '<div style="padding:16px 24px;border-bottom:1px solid #e2e8f0;background:#f0fdf4;"><strong style="font-size:0.8rem;letter-spacing:1px;color:#16a34a;text-transform:uppercase;">Near You — ' + city + '</strong></div>';
                html += '<table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;font-size:0.9rem;">';
                html += '<thead><tr style="background:#f8fafc;"><th style="padding:10px 24px;text-align:left;font-size:0.78rem;color:#94a3b8;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.5px;">Material</th><th style="padding:10px 24px;text-align:left;font-size:0.78rem;color:#94a3b8;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.5px;">Posted (USD/kg)</th><th style="padding:10px 24px;text-align:left;font-size:0.78rem;color:#94a3b8;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.5px;">GHS/kg</th><th style="padding:10px 24px;text-align:left;font-size:0.78rem;color:#94a3b8;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.5px;">Actual avg (30d)</th><th style="padding:10px 24px;text-align:left;font-size:0.78rem;color:#94a3b8;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.5px;">Buyer</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
                near.forEach(function(p) {
                    var ghsDisplay = p.price_per_kg_ghs ? 'GHS ' + parseFloat(p.price_per_kg_ghs).toFixed(2) : '—';
                    var actualAvg = p.actual_avg_price_30d ? 'GHS ' + parseFloat(p.actual_avg_price_30d).toFixed(2) : '—';
                    html += '<tr style="border-bottom:1px solid #f1f5f9;"><td style="padding:12px 24px;font-weight:600;color:#0a2e1a;">' + p.material_type + '</td><td style="padding:12px 24px;">$' + parseFloat(p.price_per_kg_usd).toFixed(4) + '</td><td style="padding:12px 24px;color:#16a34a;font-weight:600;">' + ghsDisplay + '</td><td style="padding:12px 24px;color:#64748b;">' + actualAvg + '</td><td style="padding:12px 24px;color:#334155;">' + (p.operator_name || '—') + '</td></tr>';
                });
                html += '</tbody></table>';
            }
            if (national.length > 0) {
                html += '<div style="padding:16px 24px;border-top:1px solid #e2e8f0;border-bottom:1px solid #e2e8f0;background:#fafaf9;"><strong style="font-size:0.8rem;letter-spacing:1px;color:#334155;text-transform:uppercase;">National Average</strong></div>';
                html += '<table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;font-size:0.9rem;"><thead><tr style="background:#f8fafc;"><th style="padding:10px 24px;text-align:left;font-size:0.78rem;color:#94a3b8;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.5px;">Material</th><th style="padding:10px 24px;text-align:left;font-size:0.78rem;color:#94a3b8;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.5px;">Avg (USD/kg)</th><th style="padding:10px 24px;text-align:left;font-size:0.78rem;color:#94a3b8;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.5px;">Buyers posting</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
                national.forEach(function(n) {
                    html += '<tr style="border-bottom:1px solid #f1f5f9;"><td style="padding:12px 24px;font-weight:600;color:#0a2e1a;">' + n.material_type + '</td><td style="padding:12px 24px;">$' + parseFloat(n.avg_usd).toFixed(4) + '</td><td style="padding:12px 24px;color:#64748b;">' + n.buyer_count + '</td></tr>';
                });
                html += '</tbody></table>';
            }
            if (near.length === 0 && national.length === 0) {
                html = '<div style="padding:48px;text-align:center;color:#94a3b8;"><p style="font-size:1rem;margin-bottom:8px;">No prices posted yet for this selection.</p><p style="font-size:0.85rem;">Aggregators post prices after logging in.</p></div>';
            }
            container.innerHTML = html;
        }).catch(function() {
            container.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:32px;text-align:center;color:#94a3b8;">Unable to load price data.</div>';
        });
    }
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() { loadPriceWidget(); });
    </script>

    <!-- Polsia Analytics -->
    <script>
    (function() {
        var slug = 'circul';
        if (!slug) return;
        var vid = localStorage.getItem('polsia_vid');
        if (!vid) {
            vid = 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function(c) {
                var r = Math.random() * 16 | 0;
                return (c === 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3 | 0x8)).toString(16);
            });
            localStorage.setItem('polsia_vid', vid);
        }
        new Image().src = 'https://polsia.com/api/beacon/pixel?s=' + encodeURIComponent(slug) + '&v=' + encodeURIComponent(vid);
    })();
    </script>

        td { padding: 10px 14px; border-bottom: 1px solid var(--border); vertical-align: middle; }

        .price-val { font-family: 'Space Grotesk', sans-serif; font-size: 1.5rem; font-weight: 700; color: var(--green-deep); }

<!-- DASHBOARD -->

    <nav class="nav">
