<script>
var state = { operator: null };

var ROLE_ROUTES = {
    collector: '/collector-dashboard',
    aggregator: '/aggregator-dashboard',
    processor: '/processor-dashboard',
    converter: '/converter-dashboard'
};

var MAT_COLORS = { PET: '#16a34a', HDPE: '#0891b2', LDPE: '#7c3aed', PP: '#f59e0b' };

function checkAuth() {
    var saved = localStorage.getItem('circul_operator');
    if (saved) {
        try {
            state.operator = JSON.parse(saved);
            if (state.operator.role !== 'collector') {
                var route = ROLE_ROUTES[state.operator.role];
                if (route) { window.location.href = route; return; }
            }
            showDashboard();
            return;
        } catch (e) { localStorage.removeItem('circul_operator'); }
    }
    document.getElementById('loginOverlay').classList.remove('hidden');
}

function showDashboard() {
    document.getElementById('loginOverlay').classList.add('hidden');
    document.getElementById('dashboard').style.display = '';
    var op = state.operator;
    document.getElementById('navName').textContent = op.name + (op.company ? ' · ' + op.company : '');
    // Report link — try to use operator ID for now; collector ID mapping not available at login
    document.getElementById('reportLink').href = '/report?operator_id=' + op.id;
    loadStats();
}

function handleLogin(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    var phone = document.getElementById('loginPhone').value.trim();
    var pin = document.getElementById('loginPin').value.trim();
    if (!phone || !pin) return;
    var btn = document.getElementById('loginBtn');
    btn.disabled = true; btn.innerHTML = '<div class="spinner"></div>';
    document.getElementById('loginError').classList.remove('visible');
    fetch('/api/operators/login', {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ phone: phone, pin: pin })
    })
    .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
    .then(function(data) {
        if (data.success) {
            state.operator = data.operator;
            localStorage.setItem('circul_operator', JSON.stringify(data.operator));
            if (data.operator.role !== 'collector') {
                var route = ROLE_ROUTES[data.operator.role];
                if (route) { window.location.href = route; return; }
            }
            showDashboard();
        } else {
            var e = document.getElementById('loginError');
            e.textContent = data.message || 'Invalid phone or PIN';
            e.classList.add('visible');
        }
    })
    .catch(function() {
        var e = document.getElementById('loginError');
        e.textContent = 'Connection error. Please try again.';
        e.classList.add('visible');
    })
    .finally(function() { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'Log In'; });
}

function handleLogout() {
    state.operator = null;
    localStorage.removeItem('circul_operator');
    window.location.href = '/dashboard';
}

function loadStats() {
    var id = state.operator.id;
    fetch('/api/operators/' + id + '/dashboard-stats')
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            if (!data.success) return;
            var s = data.stats;
            document.getElementById('statTotalKg').textContent = fmt(s.totals.total_kg);
            document.getElementById('statEarned').textContent = fmt(s.totals.total_value);
            document.getElementById('statTxns').textContent = s.totals.total_txns;
            document.getElementById('statMonthKg').textContent = fmt(s.this_month.month_kg);
            renderMaterials(s.by_material);
            renderRecentTxns(s.payment_history);
        });
    loadPrices();
}

function renderMaterials(mats) {
    var c = document.getElementById('materialBreakdown');
    if (!mats || !mats.length) { c.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No transactions yet</div>'; return; }
    var total = mats.reduce(function(s, m) { return s + parseFloat(m.kg); }, 0);
    var max = parseFloat(mats[0].kg);
    var html = '';
    mats.forEach(function(m) {
        var kg = parseFloat(m.kg);
        var pct = total > 0 ? (kg / total * 100) : 0;
        var bw = max > 0 ? (kg / max * 100) : 0;
        var color = MAT_COLORS[m.material_type] || '#6b7280';
        html += '<div class="mat-row"><span class="mat-label">' + m.material_type + '</span><div class="mat-bar-track"><div class="mat-bar-fill" style="width:' + bw.toFixed(1) + '%;background:' + color + '"></div></div><span class="mat-kg">' + fmt(kg) + ' kg</span><span class="mat-pct">' + pct.toFixed(1) + '%</span></div>';
    });
    c.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderRecentTxns(history) {
    var tbody = document.getElementById('txnBody');
    if (!history || !history.length) { tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="empty">No transactions yet</td></tr>'; return; }
    tbody.innerHTML = history.map(function(p) {
        var statusClass = p.status === 'success' ? 'badge-green' : p.status === 'processing' ? 'badge-amber' : 'badge-gray';
        return '<tr><td>' + fmtDate(p.created_at) + '</td><td>—</td><td>—</td><td>GHS ' + fmt(p.amount) + '</td><td><span class="badge ' + statusClass + '">' + (p.status || 'unpaid') + '</span></td><td>—</td></tr>';
    }).join('');
    // If no payment history, try fetching transactions directly
    if (!history.length) fetchRecentTxns();
}

function fetchRecentTxns() {
    var id = state.operator.id;
    fetch('/api/transactions?operator_id=' + id + '&limit=20')
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            if (!data.success || !data.transactions.length) return;
            var tbody = document.getElementById('txnBody');
            tbody.innerHTML = data.transactions.map(function(t) {
                var statusClass = t.payment_status === 'paid' ? 'badge-green' : t.payment_status === 'pending' ? 'badge-amber' : 'badge-gray';
                var collector = (t.collector_first_name || '') + ' ' + (t.collector_last_name || '');
                return '<tr><td>' + fmtDate(t.transaction_date) + '</td><td><span class="badge badge-green">' + t.material_type + '</span></td><td>' + fmt(t.net_weight_kg) + '</td><td>' + (t.total_price ? 'GHS ' + fmt(t.total_price) : '—') + '</td><td><span class="badge ' + statusClass + '">' + (t.payment_status || 'unpaid') + '</span></td><td>—</td></tr>';
            }).join('');
        });
}

function loadPrices() {
    var city = state.operator.city || 'Accra';
    document.getElementById('priceCity').textContent = city;
    fetch('/api/prices?role=collector&city=' + encodeURIComponent(city))
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            var panel = document.getElementById('pricePanel');
            if (!data.success) { panel.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No prices available</div>'; return; }
            var near = data.near_prices || [];
            var national = data.national_averages || [];
            var html = '';
            if (near.length) {
                html += '<p style="font-size:0.78rem;font-weight:600;color:var(--green-primary);margin-bottom:12px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.5px;">Near you (' + city + ')</p>';
                html += '<table style="width:100%;font-size:0.85rem;border-collapse:collapse;margin-bottom:16px;">';
                html += '<thead><tr><th style="text-align:left;padding:6px 0;color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.75rem;font-weight:600;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border)">Material</th><th style="text-align:right;padding:6px 0;color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.75rem;font-weight:600;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border)">USD/kg</th><th style="text-align:right;padding:6px 0;color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.75rem;font-weight:600;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border)">GHS/kg</th><th style="text-align:right;padding:6px 0;color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.75rem;font-weight:600;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border)">Actual avg</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
                near.forEach(function(p) {
                    html += '<tr><td style="padding:8px 0;font-weight:600;color:var(--green-deep)">' + p.material_type + '</td><td style="padding:8px 0;text-align:right">$' + parseFloat(p.price_per_kg_usd).toFixed(4) + '</td><td style="padding:8px 0;text-align:right;color:var(--green-primary);font-weight:600">' + (p.price_per_kg_ghs ? 'GHS ' + parseFloat(p.price_per_kg_ghs).toFixed(2) : '—') + '</td><td style="padding:8px 0;text-align:right;color:var(--slate-light)">' + (p.actual_avg_price_30d ? 'GHS ' + parseFloat(p.actual_avg_price_30d).toFixed(2) : '—') + '</td></tr>';
                });
                html += '</tbody></table>';
            }
            if (national.length) {
                html += '<p style="font-size:0.78rem;font-weight:600;color:var(--slate-light);margin-bottom:8px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.5px;">National average</p>';
                national.forEach(function(n) {
                    html += '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:6px 0;font-size:0.85rem;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border)"><span style="font-weight:600">' + n.material_type + '</span><span style="color:var(--slate-light)">$' + parseFloat(n.avg_usd).toFixed(4) + '/kg · ' + n.buyer_count + ' buyers</span></div>';
                });
            }
            if (!near.length && !national.length) {
                html = '<div class="empty">No prices posted yet for your area</div>';
            }
            panel.innerHTML = html;
        })
        .catch(function() {
            document.getElementById('pricePanel').innerHTML = '<div class="empty">Unable to load prices</div>';
        });
}

function fmt(n) {
    var v = parseFloat(n);
    if (isNaN(v)) return '0';
    if (v >= 1000) return v.toLocaleString('en-US', { maximumFractionDigits: 1 });
    return v.toFixed(2);
}

function fmtDate(iso) {
    if (!iso) return '—';
    var d = new Date(iso);
    return d.toLocaleDateString('en-GB', { day: '2-digit', month: 'short', year: 'numeric' });
}

checkAuth();
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
var state = { operator: null, currentRatingCollectorId: null, currentRatingStar: 0, selectedTags: [] };
var MATERIALS = ['PET', 'HDPE', 'LDPE', 'PP'];
var refreshTimer = null;

var ROLE_ROUTES = {
    collector: '/collector-dashboard',
    aggregator: '/aggregator-dashboard',
    processor: '/processor-dashboard',
    converter: '/converter-dashboard'
};

function checkAuth() {
    var saved = localStorage.getItem('circul_operator');
    if (saved) {
        try {
            state.operator = JSON.parse(saved);
            if (state.operator.role !== 'aggregator') {
                var route = ROLE_ROUTES[state.operator.role];
                if (route) { window.location.href = route; return; }
            }
            showDashboard();
            return;
        } catch (e) { localStorage.removeItem('circul_operator'); }
    }
    document.getElementById('loginOverlay').classList.remove('hidden');
}

function showDashboard() {
    document.getElementById('loginOverlay').classList.add('hidden');
    document.getElementById('dashboard').style.display = '';
    var op = state.operator;
    document.getElementById('navName').textContent = op.name + (op.company ? ' · ' + op.company : '');
    loadAll();
    refreshTimer = setInterval(loadAll, 30000);
}

function handleLogin(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    var phone = document.getElementById('loginPhone').value.trim();
    var pin = document.getElementById('loginPin').value.trim();
    if (!phone || !pin) return;
    var btn = document.getElementById('loginBtn');
    btn.disabled = true; btn.innerHTML = '<div class="spinner"></div>';
    document.getElementById('loginError').classList.remove('visible');
    fetch('/api/operators/login', {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ phone: phone, pin: pin })
    })
    .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
    .then(function(data) {
        if (data.success) {
            state.operator = data.operator;
            localStorage.setItem('circul_operator', JSON.stringify(data.operator));
            if (data.operator.role !== 'aggregator') {
                var route = ROLE_ROUTES[data.operator.role];
                if (route) { window.location.href = route; return; }
            }
            showDashboard();
        } else {
            var el = document.getElementById('loginError');
            el.textContent = data.message || 'Invalid phone or PIN';
            el.classList.add('visible');
        }
    })
    .catch(function() {
        var el = document.getElementById('loginError');
        el.textContent = 'Connection error. Please try again.';
        el.classList.add('visible');
    })
    .finally(function() { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'Log In'; });
}

function handleLogout() {
    if (refreshTimer) clearInterval(refreshTimer);
    state.operator = null;
    localStorage.removeItem('circul_operator');
    window.location.href = '/dashboard';
}

function loadAll() {
    var id = state.operator.id;
    fetch('/api/operators/' + id + '/dashboard-stats')
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            if (!data.success) return;
            var s = data.stats;
            document.getElementById('statCollectors').textContent = s.active_collectors;
            document.getElementById('statPending').textContent = s.pending_payments.count;
            document.getElementById('statPendingVal').textContent = 'GHS ' + fmt(s.pending_payments.value);
            document.getElementById('statMonthKg').textContent = fmt(s.this_month.month_kg);
            document.getElementById('statTotalKg').textContent = fmt(s.totals.total_kg);
            renderPriceCards(s.posted_prices);
            renderCollectors(s.top_collectors);
            renderRatingsReceived(s.ratings);
            renderPL(s);
        });
    loadPendingTxns();
}

function renderPriceCards(prices) {
    var priceMap = {};
    (prices || []).forEach(function(p) { priceMap[p.material_type] = p; });
    var html = MATERIALS.map(function(mat) {
        var p = priceMap[mat];
        var current = p ? '$' + parseFloat(p.price_per_kg_usd).toFixed(4) : 'Not set';
        var ghs = p && p.price_per_kg_ghs ? 'GHS ' + parseFloat(p.price_per_kg_ghs).toFixed(2) : '—';
        var actual = p && p.actual_avg_price_30d ? 'Actual avg (30d): GHS ' + parseFloat(p.actual_avg_price_30d).toFixed(2) : 'No actual data yet';
        var updated = p ? 'Updated ' + fmtDate(p.posted_at) : '';
        return '<div class="price-card">' +
            '<div class="price-card-mat">' + mat + '</div>' +
            '<div class="price-card-current">' + current + '</div>' +
            '<div class="price-card-sub">' + ghs + ' · ' + updated + '</div>' +
            '<div class="price-card-actual">' + actual + '</div>' +
            '<div class="price-input-row">' +
            '<input type="number" class="price-input" id="price-usd-' + mat + '" placeholder="USD/kg" step="0.0001" min="0">' +
            '<input type="number" class="price-input" id="price-rate-' + mat + '" placeholder="Rate" step="0.01" min="0" style="width:70px">' +
            '<button class="price-post-btn" onclick="postPrice(\'' + mat + '\')">Post</button>' +
            '</div></div>';
    }).join('');
    document.getElementById('priceCards').innerHTML = html;
}

function postPrice(mat) {
    var usd = document.getElementById('price-usd-' + mat).value;
    var rate = document.getElementById('price-rate-' + mat).value;
    if (!usd || parseFloat(usd) <= 0) { alert('Enter a valid USD price'); return; }
    var ghs = (rate && parseFloat(rate) > 0) ? (parseFloat(usd) * parseFloat(rate)).toFixed(2) : null;
    fetch('/api/prices', {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ operator_id: state.operator.id, material_type: mat, price_per_kg_usd: parseFloat(usd), price_per_kg_ghs: ghs ? parseFloat(ghs) : null, usd_to_ghs_rate: rate ? parseFloat(rate) : null })
    })
    .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
    .then(function(data) { if (data.success) { loadAll(); } else { alert(data.message); } });
}

function renderCollectors(collectors) {
    var tbody = document.getElementById('collectorsBody');
    if (!collectors || !collectors.length) { tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="empty">No collectors yet</td></tr>'; return; }
    tbody.innerHTML = collectors.map(function(c) {
        var name = c.first_name + ' ' + c.last_name;
        var rating = c.average_rating ? '⭐ ' + parseFloat(c.average_rating).toFixed(1) : '—';
        return '<tr>' +
            '<td>' + esc(name) + '</td>' +
            '<td>' + esc(c.city || '—') + '</td>' +
            '<td>' + fmt(c.total_kg) + ' kg</td>' +
            '<td>' + c.txns + '</td>' +
            '<td>' + rating + '</td>' +
            '<td><button class="btn-pay" onclick="openRatingModal(' + c.id + ',\'' + esc(name) + '\')">Rate</button></td>' +
            '</tr>';
    }).join('');
}

function loadPendingTxns() {
    fetch('/api/transactions?operator_id=' + state.operator.id + '&limit=50')
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            if (!data.success) return;
            var pending = (data.transactions || []).filter(function(t) { return t.payment_status === 'unpaid' && parseFloat(t.total_price) > 0; });
            var tbody = document.getElementById('pendingBody');
            if (!pending.length) { tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="empty">No pending payments</td></tr>'; return; }
            tbody.innerHTML = pending.map(function(t) {
                var name = (t.collector_first_name || '') + ' ' + (t.collector_last_name || '');
                return '<tr>' +
                    '<td>' + fmtDate(t.transaction_date) + '</td>' +
                    '<td>' + esc(name.trim()) + '</td>' +
                    '<td><span class="badge badge-green">' + t.material_type + '</span></td>' +
                    '<td>' + fmt(t.net_weight_kg) + '</td>' +
                    '<td>GHS ' + fmt(t.total_price) + '</td>' +
                    '<td><span class="badge badge-amber">Unpaid</span></td>' +
                    '</tr>';
            }).join('');
        });
}

function renderPL(s) {
    var paid = (s.payment_history || []).filter(function(p) { return p.status === 'success'; }).reduce(function(acc, p) { return acc + parseFloat(p.amount || 0); }, 0);
    document.getElementById('plSummary').innerHTML =
        '<div class="stat-card"><div class="stat-label">Total purchased (GHS)</div><div class="stat-value">' + fmt(s.totals.total_value) + '</div></div>' +
        '<div class="stat-card"><div class="stat-label">Total paid out (GHS)</div><div class="stat-value">' + fmt(paid) + '</div></div>' +
        '<div class="stat-card"><div class="stat-label">Outstanding (GHS)</div><div class="stat-value warn">' + fmt(s.pending_payments.value) + '</div></div>' +
        '<div class="stat-card"><div class="stat-label">This month (GHS)</div><div class="stat-value">' + fmt(s.this_month.month_value) + '</div></div>';
}

function renderRatingsReceived(ratings) {
    var el = document.getElementById('ratingsReceivedList');
    if (!ratings || !ratings.avg_rating) { el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No ratings received yet</div>'; return; }
    el.innerHTML = '<div style="font-size:1.4rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--green-deep)">⭐ ' + ratings.avg_rating + ' <span style="font-size:0.85rem;color:var(--slate-light);font-weight:400">from ' + ratings.count + ' ratings</span></div>';
}

// RATING MODAL
function openRatingModal(collectorId, name) {
    state.currentRatingCollectorId = collectorId;
    state.currentRatingStar = 0;
    state.selectedTags = [];
    document.getElementById('ratingCollectorName').textContent = name;
    document.querySelectorAll('.star').forEach(function(s) { s.classList.remove('lit'); });
    document.querySelectorAll('.tag-chip').forEach(function(c) { c.classList.remove('selected-pos', 'selected-neg'); });
    document.getElementById('ratingNote').value = '';
    document.getElementById('submitRatingBtn').disabled = true;
    document.getElementById('ratingModal').classList.add('open');
}

function closeRatingModal() { document.getElementById('ratingModal').classList.remove('open'); }

function setStar(n) {
    state.currentRatingStar = n;
    document.querySelectorAll('.star').forEach(function(s) {
        s.classList.toggle('lit', parseInt(s.getAttribute('data-r')) <= n);
    });
    document.getElementById('submitRatingBtn').disabled = false;
}

function toggleTag(chip) {
    var tag = chip.getAttribute('data-tag');
    var type = chip.getAttribute('data-type');
    var idx = state.selectedTags.indexOf(tag);
    if (idx >= 0) { state.selectedTags.splice(idx, 1); chip.classList.remove('selected-pos', 'selected-neg'); }
    else { state.selectedTags.push(tag); chip.classList.add(type === 'pos' ? 'selected-pos' : 'selected-neg'); }
}

function submitRating() {
    if (!state.currentRatingStar) return;
    fetch('/api/ratings/operator', {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
            rater_operator_id: state.operator.id,
            rated_collector_id: state.currentRatingCollectorId,
            rating: state.currentRatingStar,
            tags: state.selectedTags,
            notes: document.getElementById('ratingNote').value || null,
            rating_direction: 'aggregator_rates_collector'
        })
    })
    .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
    .then(function(data) { if (data.success) { closeRatingModal(); } else { alert(data.message); } });
}

document.getElementById('ratingModal').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    if (e.target === this) closeRatingModal();
});

function fmt(n) {
    var v = parseFloat(n);
    if (isNaN(v)) return '0';
    if (v >= 10000) return v.toLocaleString('en-US', { maximumFractionDigits: 0 });
    if (v >= 100) return v.toLocaleString('en-US', { maximumFractionDigits: 1 });
    return v.toFixed(2);
}

function fmtDate(iso) {
    if (!iso) return '—';
    return new Date(iso).toLocaleDateString('en-GB', { day: '2-digit', month: 'short', year: 'numeric' });
}

function esc(s) {
    var d = document.createElement('div'); d.textContent = s || ''; return d.innerHTML;
}

checkAuth();
</script>
</body>
</html>


===== FILE: public/processor-dashboard.html =====

<script>
var state = { operator: null };
var MATERIALS = ['PET', 'HDPE', 'LDPE', 'PP'];
var ROLE_ROUTES = { collector: '/collector-dashboard', aggregator: '/aggregator-dashboard', processor: '/processor-dashboard', converter: '/converter-dashboard' };

function checkAuth() {
    var saved = localStorage.getItem('circul_operator');
    if (saved) {
        try {
            state.operator = JSON.parse(saved);
            if (state.operator.role !== 'processor') {
                var route = ROLE_ROUTES[state.operator.role];
                if (route) { window.location.href = route; return; }
            }
            showDashboard();
            return;
        } catch (e) { localStorage.removeItem('circul_operator'); }
    }
    document.getElementById('loginOverlay').classList.remove('hidden');
}

function showDashboard() {
    document.getElementById('loginOverlay').classList.add('hidden');
    document.getElementById('dashboard').style.display = '';
    var op = state.operator;
    var title = 'Processor';
    if (op.company && op.company.toLowerCase().indexOf('repatrn') >= 0) title = 'rePATRN — Processor';
    document.getElementById('navTitle').textContent = title;
    document.getElementById('navName').textContent = op.name + (op.company ? ' · ' + op.company : '');
    loadAll();
}

function handleLogin(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    var phone = document.getElementById('loginPhone').value.trim();
    var pin = document.getElementById('loginPin').value.trim();
    if (!phone || !pin) return;
    var btn = document.getElementById('loginBtn');
    btn.disabled = true; btn.innerHTML = '<div class="spinner"></div>';
    document.getElementById('loginError').classList.remove('visible');
    fetch('/api/operators/login', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ phone: phone, pin: pin }) })
    .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
    .then(function(data) {
        if (data.success) {
            state.operator = data.operator;
            localStorage.setItem('circul_operator', JSON.stringify(data.operator));
            if (data.operator.role !== 'processor') {
                var route = ROLE_ROUTES[data.operator.role];
                if (route) { window.location.href = route; return; }
            }
            showDashboard();
        } else {
            var el = document.getElementById('loginError');
            el.textContent = data.message || 'Invalid phone or PIN';
            el.classList.add('visible');
        }
    })
    .catch(function() {
        var el = document.getElementById('loginError'); el.textContent = 'Connection error.'; el.classList.add('visible');
    })
    .finally(function() { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'Log In'; });
}

function handleLogout() {
    state.operator = null; localStorage.removeItem('circul_operator'); window.location.href = '/dashboard';
}

function loadAll() {
    var id = state.operator.id;
    fetch('/api/operators/' + id + '/dashboard-stats')
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            if (!data.success) return;
            var s = data.stats;
            document.getElementById('statMonthKg').textContent = fmt(s.this_month.month_kg);
            document.getElementById('statTxns').textContent = s.totals.total_txns;
            document.getElementById('statPending').textContent = fmt(s.pending_payments.value);
            document.getElementById('statTotal').textContent = fmt(s.totals.total_kg);
            renderPriceCards(s.posted_prices);
        });
    loadTxns();
    loadAggregators();
}

function loadTxns() {
    fetch('/api/transactions?operator_id=' + state.operator.id + '&limit=30')
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            var tbody = document.getElementById('supplyBody');
            if (!data.success || !data.transactions.length) { tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="empty">No transactions yet</td></tr>'; return; }
            tbody.innerHTML = data.transactions.map(function(t) {
                var statusClass = t.payment_status === 'paid' ? 'badge-green' : t.payment_status === 'pending' ? 'badge-amber' : 'badge-gray';
                var gps = t.lat ? '<span class="badge badge-green">GPS ✓</span>' : '<span class="badge badge-gray">—</span>';
                return '<tr>' +
                    '<td>' + fmtDate(t.transaction_date) + '</td>' +
                    '<td><span class="badge badge-blue">' + t.material_type + '</span></td>' +
                    '<td>' + fmt(t.net_weight_kg) + ' kg</td>' +
                    '<td>' + (t.total_price ? 'GHS ' + fmt(t.total_price) : '—') + '</td>' +
                    '<td><span class="badge ' + statusClass + '">' + (t.payment_status || 'unpaid') + '</span></td>' +
                    '<td>' + gps + '</td>' +
                    '</tr>';
            }).join('');
        });
}

function loadAggregators() {
    fetch('/api/transactions?operator_id=' + state.operator.id + '&limit=100')
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            var el = document.getElementById('aggregatorRatingsList');
            if (!data.success || !data.transactions.length) { el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No transactions yet</div>'; return; }
            // Unique aggregators from transactions
            var seen = {};
            data.transactions.forEach(function(t) {
                if (t.operator_id && t.operator_name && !seen[t.operator_id]) seen[t.operator_id] = t.operator_name;
            });
            var aggs = Object.keys(seen);
            if (!aggs.length) { el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No aggregators to rate yet</div>'; return; }
            el.innerHTML = '<table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;font-size:0.88rem;"><thead><tr><th style="padding:8px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);text-align:left;color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.75rem;text-transform:uppercase">Aggregator</th><th style="padding:8px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border)"></th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
                aggs.map(function(id) {
                    return '<tr><td style="padding:10px 0">' + esc(seen[id]) + '</td><td style="padding:10px 0;text-align:right"><button onclick="rateAggregator(' + id + ',\'' + esc(seen[id]) + '\')" style="padding:6px 14px;background:var(--green-primary);color:white;border:none;border-radius:6px;font-family:\'Space Grotesk\',sans-serif;font-size:0.78rem;font-weight:600;cursor:pointer">Rate</button></td></tr>';
                }).join('') + '</tbody></table>';
        });
}

function rateAggregator(aggId, name) {
    var r = prompt('Rate ' + name + ' (1-5 stars):');
    if (!r || isNaN(parseInt(r)) || parseInt(r) < 1 || parseInt(r) > 5) return;
    fetch('/api/ratings/operator', {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ rater_operator_id: state.operator.id, rated_operator_id: aggId, rating: parseInt(r), rating_direction: 'processor_rates_aggregator' })
    }).then(function(r) { return r.json(); }).then(function(d) { if (d.success) alert('Rating submitted!'); });
}

function renderPriceCards(prices) {
    var priceMap = {};
    (prices || []).forEach(function(p) { priceMap[p.material_type] = p; });
    document.getElementById('priceCards').innerHTML = MATERIALS.map(function(mat) {
        var p = priceMap[mat];
        var current = p ? '$' + parseFloat(p.price_per_kg_usd).toFixed(4) : 'Not set';
        return '<div class="price-card">' +
            '<div class="price-card-mat">' + mat + '</div>' +
            '<div class="price-card-current">' + current + '</div>' +
            '<div class="price-input-row">' +
            '<input type="number" class="price-input" id="price-usd-' + mat + '" placeholder="USD/kg" step="0.0001" min="0">' +
            '<input type="number" class="price-input" id="price-rate-' + mat + '" placeholder="Rate" step="0.01" min="0" style="width:70px">' +
            '<button class="price-post-btn" onclick="postPrice(\'' + mat + '\')">Post</button>' +
            '</div></div>';
    }).join('');
}

function postPrice(mat) {
    var usd = document.getElementById('price-usd-' + mat).value;
    var rate = document.getElementById('price-rate-' + mat).value;
    if (!usd || parseFloat(usd) <= 0) { alert('Enter a valid USD price'); return; }
    var ghs = (rate && parseFloat(rate) > 0) ? (parseFloat(usd) * parseFloat(rate)).toFixed(2) : null;
    fetch('/api/prices', {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ operator_id: state.operator.id, material_type: mat, price_per_kg_usd: parseFloat(usd), price_per_kg_ghs: ghs ? parseFloat(ghs) : null, usd_to_ghs_rate: rate ? parseFloat(rate) : null })
    }).then(function(r) { return r.json(); }).then(function(data) { if (data.success) loadAll(); else alert(data.message); });
}

function downloadCompliance(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    window.location.href = '/api/reports/compliance/' + state.operator.id + '?format=json';
}

function fmt(n) { var v = parseFloat(n); if (isNaN(v)) return '0'; if (v >= 10000) return v.toLocaleString('en-US', { maximumFractionDigits: 0 }); if (v >= 100) return v.toLocaleString('en-US', { maximumFractionDigits: 1 }); return v.toFixed(2); }
function fmtDate(iso) { if (!iso) return '—'; return new Date(iso).toLocaleDateString('en-GB', { day: '2-digit', month: 'short', year: 'numeric' }); }
function esc(s) { var d = document.createElement('div'); d.textContent = s || ''; return d.innerHTML; }

checkAuth();
</script>
</body>
</html>


===== FILE: public/converter-dashboard.html =====

<script>
var state = { operator: null };
var MATERIALS = ['PET', 'HDPE', 'LDPE', 'PP'];
var ROLE_ROUTES = { collector: '/collector-dashboard', aggregator: '/aggregator-dashboard', processor: '/processor-dashboard', converter: '/converter-dashboard' };

function checkAuth() {
    var saved = localStorage.getItem('circul_operator');
    if (saved) {
        try {
            state.operator = JSON.parse(saved);
            if (state.operator.role !== 'converter') {
                var route = ROLE_ROUTES[state.operator.role];
                if (route) { window.location.href = route; return; }
            }
            showDashboard();
            return;
        } catch (e) { localStorage.removeItem('circul_operator'); }
    }
    document.getElementById('loginOverlay').classList.remove('hidden');
}

function showDashboard() {
    document.getElementById('loginOverlay').classList.add('hidden');
    document.getElementById('dashboard').style.display = '';
    var op = state.operator;
    document.getElementById('navName').textContent = op.name + (op.company ? ' · ' + op.company : '');
    loadAll();
}

function handleLogin(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    var phone = document.getElementById('loginPhone').value.trim();
    var pin = document.getElementById('loginPin').value.trim();
    if (!phone || !pin) return;
    var btn = document.getElementById('loginBtn');
    btn.disabled = true; btn.innerHTML = '<div class="spinner"></div>';
    document.getElementById('loginError').classList.remove('visible');
    fetch('/api/operators/login', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ phone: phone, pin: pin }) })
    .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
    .then(function(data) {
        if (data.success) {
            state.operator = data.operator;
            localStorage.setItem('circul_operator', JSON.stringify(data.operator));
            if (data.operator.role !== 'converter') {
                var route = ROLE_ROUTES[data.operator.role];
                if (route) { window.location.href = route; return; }
            }
            showDashboard();
        } else {
            var el = document.getElementById('loginError'); el.textContent = data.message || 'Invalid phone or PIN'; el.classList.add('visible');
        }
    })
    .catch(function() { var el = document.getElementById('loginError'); el.textContent = 'Connection error.'; el.classList.add('visible'); })
    .finally(function() { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'Log In'; });
}

function handleLogout() {
    state.operator = null; localStorage.removeItem('circul_operator'); window.location.href = '/dashboard';
}

function showTab(tab, el) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(function(t) { t.classList.remove('active'); });
    el.classList.add('active');
    document.querySelectorAll('.tab-panel').forEach(function(p) { p.classList.remove('active'); });
    document.getElementById('tab-' + tab).classList.add('active');
    if (tab === 'prices') loadProcessorPrices();
    if (tab === 'certs') loadTxnCerts();
    if (tab === 'ratings') loadRatings();
}

function loadAll() {
    var id = state.operator.id;
    fetch('/api/operators/' + id + '/dashboard-stats')
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            if (!data.success) return;
            var s = data.stats;
            document.getElementById('statTxns').textContent = s.totals.total_txns;
            document.getElementById('statTotalKg').textContent = fmt(s.totals.total_kg) + ' kg';
            document.getElementById('statPending').textContent = fmt(s.pending_payments.value);
            renderPriceCards(s.posted_prices);
        });
    loadTxns();
}

function loadTxns() {
    fetch('/api/transactions?operator_id=' + state.operator.id + '&limit=30')
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            var tbody = document.getElementById('supplyBody');
            // Count unique processors
            var uniqueProcs = new Set();
            if (data.success && data.transactions) {
                data.transactions.forEach(function(t) { if (t.operator_id) uniqueProcs.add(t.operator_id); });
                document.getElementById('statProcessors').textContent = uniqueProcs.size;
            }
            if (!data.success || !data.transactions.length) { tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="7" class="empty">No transactions yet</td></tr>'; return; }
            tbody.innerHTML = data.transactions.map(function(t) {
                var sc = t.payment_status === 'paid' ? 'badge-green' : t.payment_status === 'pending' ? 'badge-amber' : 'badge-gray';
                var gps = t.lat ? '<span class="badge badge-green">GPS ✓</span>' : '—';
                var journey = '<a href="/api/reports/product-journey/' + t.id + '" target="_blank" style="font-size:0.78rem;color:var(--green-primary)">View</a>';
                return '<tr><td>' + fmtDate(t.transaction_date) + '</td><td><span class="badge badge-blue">' + t.material_type + '</span></td><td>' + fmt(t.net_weight_kg) + ' kg</td><td>' + (t.total_price ? 'GHS ' + fmt(t.total_price) : '—') + '</td><td><span class="badge ' + sc + '">' + (t.payment_status || 'unpaid') + '</span></td><td>' + gps + '</td><td>' + journey + '</td></tr>';
            }).join('');
        });
}

function loadProcessorPrices() {
    var city = state.operator.city || '';
    document.getElementById('priceCity').textContent = city || 'National';
    fetch('/api/prices?role=converter' + (city ? '&city=' + encodeURIComponent(city) : ''))
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            var el = document.getElementById('processorPrices');
            var all = data.all_prices || [];
            if (!all.length) { el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No processor prices posted yet</div>'; return; }
            el.innerHTML = '<table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;font-size:0.88rem;"><thead><tr><th style="padding:10px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.75rem;text-transform:uppercase">Material</th><th style="padding:10px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.75rem;text-transform:uppercase">USD/kg</th><th style="padding:10px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.75rem;text-transform:uppercase">GHS/kg</th><th style="padding:10px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.75rem;text-transform:uppercase">Processor</th><th style="padding:10px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.75rem;text-transform:uppercase">City</th><th style="padding:10px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.75rem;text-transform:uppercase">Actual avg</th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
                all.map(function(p) {
                    return '<tr><td style="padding:10px 0;font-weight:600">' + p.material_type + '</td><td style="padding:10px 0">$' + parseFloat(p.price_per_kg_usd).toFixed(4) + '</td><td style="padding:10px 0;color:var(--green-primary);font-weight:600">' + (p.price_per_kg_ghs ? 'GHS ' + parseFloat(p.price_per_kg_ghs).toFixed(2) : '—') + '</td><td style="padding:10px 0">' + esc(p.operator_name || '—') + '</td><td style="padding:10px 0">' + esc(p.city || '—') + '</td><td style="padding:10px 0;color:var(--slate-light)">' + (p.actual_avg_price_30d ? 'GHS ' + parseFloat(p.actual_avg_price_30d).toFixed(2) : '—') + '</td></tr>';
                }).join('') + '</tbody></table>';
        });
}

function loadTxnCerts() {
    fetch('/api/transactions?operator_id=' + state.operator.id + '&limit=20')
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            var el = document.getElementById('txnCerts');
            if (!data.success || !data.transactions.length) { el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No transactions yet</div>'; return; }
            el.innerHTML = '<table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;font-size:0.88rem;"><thead><tr><th style="padding:8px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);text-align:left;color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.75rem;text-transform:uppercase">Date</th><th style="padding:8px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);text-align:left;color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.75rem;text-transform:uppercase">Material</th><th style="padding:8px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);text-align:left;color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.75rem;text-transform:uppercase">kg</th><th style="padding:8px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);text-align:left;color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.75rem;text-transform:uppercase">Actions</th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
                data.transactions.map(function(t) {
                    return '<tr><td style="padding:10px 0">' + fmtDate(t.transaction_date) + '</td><td style="padding:10px 0"><span class="badge badge-blue">' + t.material_type + '</span></td><td style="padding:10px 0">' + fmt(t.net_weight_kg) + ' kg</td><td style="padding:10px 0"><a href="/api/reports/product-journey/' + t.id + '" target="_blank" style="color:var(--green-primary);font-size:0.8rem;margin-right:12px">Journey QR</a></td></tr>';
                }).join('') + '</tbody></table>';
        });
}

function loadRatings() {
    fetch('/api/transactions?operator_id=' + state.operator.id + '&limit=100')
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            var el = document.getElementById('processorRatingsList');
            if (!data.success || !data.transactions.length) { el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No transactions yet</div>'; return; }
            var seen = {};
            data.transactions.forEach(function(t) { if (t.operator_id && t.operator_name && !seen[t.operator_id]) seen[t.operator_id] = t.operator_name; });
            var procs = Object.keys(seen);
            if (!procs.length) { el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No processors to rate yet</div>'; return; }
            el.innerHTML = procs.map(function(id) {
                return '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;padding:12px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border)"><span>' + esc(seen[id]) + '</span><button onclick="rateProcessor(' + id + ',\'' + esc(seen[id]) + '\')" style="padding:6px 14px;background:var(--green-primary);color:white;border:none;border-radius:6px;font-family:\'Space Grotesk\',sans-serif;font-size:0.78rem;font-weight:600;cursor:pointer">Rate</button></div>';
            }).join('');
        });
    fetch('/api/ratings/operator/' + state.operator.id)
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            var el = document.getElementById('ratingsReceived');
            if (!data.success || !data.ratings.length) { el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No ratings received yet</div>'; return; }
            el.innerHTML = '<div style="font-size:1.4rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--green-deep);margin-bottom:12px">⭐ ' + (data.summary.avg_rating || '—') + ' <span style="font-size:0.85rem;color:var(--slate-light);font-weight:400">from ' + data.summary.count + ' ratings</span></div>';
        });
}

function rateProcessor(procId, name) {
    var r = prompt('Rate ' + name + ' (1-5):');
    if (!r || isNaN(parseInt(r)) || parseInt(r) < 1 || parseInt(r) > 5) return;
    fetch('/api/ratings/operator', {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ rater_operator_id: state.operator.id, rated_operator_id: procId, rating: parseInt(r), rating_direction: 'converter_rates_processor' })
    }).then(function(r) { return r.json(); }).then(function(d) { if (d.success) alert('Rating submitted!'); });
}

function renderPriceCards(prices) {
    var priceMap = {};
    (prices || []).forEach(function(p) { priceMap[p.material_type] = p; });
    document.getElementById('priceCards').innerHTML = MATERIALS.map(function(mat) {
        var p = priceMap[mat];
        var current = p ? '$' + parseFloat(p.price_per_kg_usd).toFixed(4) : 'Not set';
        return '<div class="price-card"><div class="price-card-mat">' + mat + '</div><div class="price-card-current">' + current + '</div><div class="price-input-row"><input type="number" class="price-input" id="price-usd-' + mat + '" placeholder="USD/kg" step="0.0001" min="0"><input type="number" class="price-input" id="price-rate-' + mat + '" placeholder="Rate" step="0.01" min="0" style="width:70px"><button class="price-post-btn" onclick="postPrice(\'' + mat + '\')">Post</button></div></div>';
    }).join('');
}

function postPrice(mat) {
    var usd = document.getElementById('price-usd-' + mat).value;
    var rate = document.getElementById('price-rate-' + mat).value;
    if (!usd || parseFloat(usd) <= 0) { alert('Enter a valid USD price'); return; }
    var ghs = (rate && parseFloat(rate) > 0) ? (parseFloat(usd) * parseFloat(rate)).toFixed(2) : null;
    fetch('/api/prices', {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ operator_id: state.operator.id, material_type: mat, price_per_kg_usd: parseFloat(usd), price_per_kg_ghs: ghs ? parseFloat(ghs) : null, usd_to_ghs_rate: rate ? parseFloat(rate) : null })
    }).then(function(r) { return r.json(); }).then(function(data) { if (data.success) loadAll(); else alert(data.message); });
}

function downloadCompliance(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    window.location.href = '/api/reports/compliance/' + state.operator.id + '?format=json';
}

function fmt(n) { var v = parseFloat(n); if (isNaN(v)) return '0'; if (v >= 10000) return v.toLocaleString('en-US', { maximumFractionDigits: 0 }); if (v >= 100) return v.toLocaleString('en-US', { maximumFractionDigits: 1 }); return v.toFixed(2); }
function fmtDate(iso) { if (!iso) return '—'; return new Date(iso).toLocaleDateString('en-GB', { day: '2-digit', month: 'short', year: 'numeric' }); }
function esc(s) { var d = document.createElement('div'); d.textContent = s || ''; return d.innerHTML; }

checkAuth();
</script>
</body>
</html>


===== FILE: public/report.html =====

<script>
var passportData = null;
var MAT_COLORS = { PET: '#16a34a', HDPE: '#0891b2', LDPE: '#7c3aed', PP: '#f59e0b' };

function getParam(name) {
    var url = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    return url.get(name);
}

function init() {
    var collectorId = getParam('id');
    var operatorId = getParam('operator_id');

    if (collectorId) {
        loadPassport(collectorId);
    } else if (operatorId) {
        // Try to find collector linked to this operator by looking up their transactions
        fetchCollectorForOperator(operatorId);
    } else {
        // Try from localStorage
        var saved = localStorage.getItem('circul_collector');
        if (saved) {
            try {
                var c = JSON.parse(saved);
                if (c.id) { loadPassport(c.id); return; }
            } catch (e) {}
        }
        showError('No collector ID provided. Add ?id=COLLECTOR_ID to the URL.');
    }
}

function fetchCollectorForOperator(opId) {
    // Look up transactions for this operator and find first collector
    fetch('/api/transactions?operator_id=' + opId + '&limit=1')
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            if (data.success && data.transactions && data.transactions.length) {
                loadPassport(data.transactions[0].collector_id);
            } else {
                showError('No transaction history found for this account. Log your first collection to build your passport.');
            }
        })
        .catch(function() { showError('Unable to load passport data.'); });
}

function loadPassport(id) {
    fetch('/api/collectors/' + id + '/passport')
        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            if (!data.success) { showError(data.message || 'Passport not found'); return; }
            passportData = data.passport;
            renderPassport(data.passport);
        })
        .catch(function() { showError('Unable to load collector passport. Please try again.'); });
}

function renderPassport(p) {
    document.getElementById('loadingScreen').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('passportContent').style.display = '';
    document.getElementById('passportFooter').style.display = '';

    // Header
    var c = p.collector;
    document.getElementById('collectorName').textContent = c.first_name + ' ' + (c.last_name || '');
    document.getElementById('activeSince').textContent = p.active_since ? fmtDate(p.active_since) : 'N/A';
    document.getElementById('collectorCity').textContent = c.city || c.region || '—';
    document.getElementById('collectorRegion').textContent = c.region || '—';

    // Stats
    document.getElementById('statTotalKg').textContent = fmt(p.total_kg_lifetime) + ' kg';
    document.getElementById('statKg12m').textContent = fmt(p.total_kg_last_12m) + ' kg';
    document.getElementById('statEarned').textContent = fmt(p.total_earned_ghs);
    document.getElementById('statTxns').textContent = p.transaction_count;

    // Ratings
    var rEl = document.getElementById('ratingsDisplay');
    if (p.avg_rating_from_aggregators && p.ratings_count > 0) {
        var stars = '';
        for (var i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {
            var lit = i <= Math.round(parseFloat(p.avg_rating_from_aggregators));
            stars += '<div class="star-icon' + (lit ? '' : ' empty') + '"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M12 2l3.09 6.26L22 9.27l-5 4.87 1.18 6.88L12 17.77l-6.18 3.25L7 14.14 2 9.27l6.91-1.01L12 2z"/></svg></div>';
        }
        rEl.innerHTML = '<div class="rating-display"><div class="stars-display">' + stars + '</div><span style="font-family:\'Space Grotesk\',sans-serif;font-size:1.2rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--green-deep);margin-left:8px">' + p.avg_rating_from_aggregators + '</span><span style="color:var(--slate-light);font-size:0.85rem;margin-left:4px">from ' + p.ratings_count + ' ratings</span></div>';
    } else {
        rEl.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No ratings from aggregators yet</div>';
    }

    // Material breakdown
    var mEl = document.getElementById('materialBreakdown');
    if (!p.material_breakdown || !p.material_breakdown.length) { mEl.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No transactions yet</div>'; }
    else {
        var total = p.material_breakdown.reduce(function(s, m) { return s + parseFloat(m.kg || 0); }, 0);
        var max = parseFloat(p.material_breakdown[0].kg || 0);
        mEl.innerHTML = p.material_breakdown.map(function(m) {
            var kg = parseFloat(m.kg || 0);
            var pct = total > 0 ? (kg / total * 100) : 0;
            var bw = max > 0 ? (kg / max * 100) : 0;
            var color = MAT_COLORS[m.material_type] || '#6b7280';
            return '<div class="mat-row"><span class="mat-label">' + m.material_type + '</span><div class="mat-track"><div class="mat-fill" style="width:' + bw.toFixed(1) + '%;background:' + color + '"></div></div><span class="mat-kg">' + fmt(kg) + ' kg</span><span class="mat-pct">' + pct.toFixed(1) + '%</span></div>';
        }).join('');
    }

    // Aggregators
    var aEl = document.getElementById('aggregatorsList');
    if (!p.aggregators_transacted_with || !p.aggregators_transacted_with.length) { aEl.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No aggregators yet</div>'; }
    else {
        aEl.innerHTML = '<div class="agg-list">' + p.aggregators_transacted_with.map(function(a) {
            var initials = (a.name || 'A').slice(0, 2).toUpperCase();
            return '<div class="agg-item"><div class="agg-icon">' + esc(initials) + '</div><div class="agg-info"><div class="agg-name">' + esc(a.name) + '</div><div class="agg-meta">' + esc(a.company || '') + (a.city ? ' · ' + esc(a.city) : '') + '</div></div></div>';
        }).join('') + '</div>';
    }

    // Recent transactions
    var tbody = document.getElementById('txnBody');
    if (!p.recent_transactions || !p.recent_transactions.length) { tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="empty">No transactions yet</td></tr>'; }
    else {
        tbody.innerHTML = p.recent_transactions.map(function(t) {
            var sc = t.payment_status === 'paid' ? 'badge-green' : t.payment_status === 'pending' ? 'badge-amber' : 'badge-gray';
            return '<tr><td>' + fmtDate(t.transaction_date) + '</td><td><span class="badge badge-green">' + t.material_type + '</span></td><td>' + fmt(t.net_weight_kg) + ' kg</td><td>' + (t.total_price ? 'GHS ' + fmt(t.total_price) : '—') + '</td><td><span class="badge ' + sc + '">' + (t.payment_status || 'unpaid') + '</span></td></tr>';
        }).join('');
    }
}

function showError(msg) {
    document.getElementById('loadingScreen').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('errorContent').style.display = '';
    document.getElementById('errorMsg').textContent = msg;
}

function downloadJSON() {
    if (!passportData) return;
    var blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(passportData, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
    var url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    var a = document.createElement('a');
    var name = (passportData.collector.first_name + '-' + (passportData.collector.last_name || 'passport')).toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-');
    a.href = url; a.download = 'circul-passport-' + name + '.json'; a.click();
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
}

function fmt(n) { var v = parseFloat(n); if (isNaN(v)) return '0'; if (v >= 1000) return v.toLocaleString('en-US', { maximumFractionDigits: 1 }); return v.toFixed(2); }
function fmtDate(iso) { if (!iso) return '—'; return new Date(iso).toLocaleDateString('en-GB', { day: '2-digit', month: 'short', year: 'numeric' }); }
function esc(s) { var d = document.createElement('div'); d.textContent = s || ''; return d.innerHTML; }

init();
</script>
</body>
</html>

/**
 * Expand schema for multi-role platform:
 * - Expand operators.role to include collector, aggregator, processor, converter
 * - Add location fields to operators and collectors
 * - Create posted_prices table (self-posted by aggregators/processors)
 * - Rebuild ratings table to support all role pairs
 * - Create collector_passports table
 * - Seed demo operators for all roles
 * - Seed demo collectors
 */

module.exports = {
  name: 'expand_schema',
  up: async (client) => {

    // 1. Expand operators.role constraint
    await client.query(`ALTER TABLE operators DROP CONSTRAINT IF EXISTS operators_role_check`);
    await client.query(`ALTER TABLE operators ADD CONSTRAINT operators_role_check CHECK (role IN ('operator','admin','collector','aggregator','processor','converter'))`);

    // 2. Add location and flag fields to operators
    await client.query(`ALTER TABLE operators ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS city VARCHAR(100)`);
    await client.query(`ALTER TABLE operators ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS region VARCHAR(100)`);
    await client.query(`ALTER TABLE operators ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS country VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT 'Ghana'`);
    await client.query(`ALTER TABLE operators ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS is_flagged BOOLEAN DEFAULT false`);

    // 3. Add location fields to collectors
    await client.query(`ALTER TABLE collectors ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS city VARCHAR(100)`);

    // 4. Create posted_prices table
    await client.query(`
      CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS posted_prices (
        id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
        operator_id INTEGER NOT NULL REFERENCES operators(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
        material_type VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL CHECK (material_type IN ('PET','HDPE','LDPE','PP')),
        price_per_kg_usd NUMERIC(10,4) NOT NULL CHECK (price_per_kg_usd >= 0),
        price_per_kg_ghs NUMERIC(10,2),
        usd_to_ghs_rate NUMERIC(10,4),
        city VARCHAR(100),
        region VARCHAR(100),
        country VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT 'Ghana',
        expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
        is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
        posted_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
        UNIQUE(operator_id, material_type, expires_at)
      )
    `);
    await client.query(`CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_posted_prices_material ON posted_prices(material_type)`);
    await client.query(`CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_posted_prices_city ON posted_prices(city)`);
    await client.query(`CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_posted_prices_expires ON posted_prices(expires_at)`);

    // 5. Rebuild ratings table to support all role pairs
    await client.query(`DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ratings CASCADE`);
    await client.query(`
      CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ratings (
        id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
        transaction_id INTEGER REFERENCES transactions(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
        rater_operator_id INTEGER REFERENCES operators(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
        rated_operator_id INTEGER REFERENCES operators(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
        rater_collector_id INTEGER REFERENCES collectors(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
        rated_collector_id INTEGER REFERENCES collectors(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
        rating INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK (rating >= 1 AND rating <= 5),
        tags JSONB DEFAULT '[]'::jsonb,
        notes TEXT,
        rating_direction VARCHAR(50),
        created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
        window_expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
        CONSTRAINT one_rating_per_transaction_direction UNIQUE (transaction_id, rater_operator_id, rated_operator_id)
      )
    `);
    await client.query(`CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ratings_rated_operator ON ratings(rated_operator_id)`);
    await client.query(`CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ratings_rater_operator ON ratings(rater_operator_id)`);
    await client.query(`CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ratings_transaction ON ratings(transaction_id)`);

    // 6. Create collector_passports table
    await client.query(`
      CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS collector_passports (
        collector_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY REFERENCES collectors(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
        total_kg_lifetime NUMERIC(12,2) DEFAULT 0,
        total_kg_last_12m NUMERIC(12,2) DEFAULT 0,
        total_earned_ghs NUMERIC(12,2) DEFAULT 0,
        total_earned_usd NUMERIC(12,2) DEFAULT 0,
        transaction_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        active_since TIMESTAMPTZ,
        material_breakdown JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
        unique_aggregators INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        avg_rating_from_aggregators NUMERIC(3,2),
        payment_reliability_score NUMERIC(5,2),
        last_updated TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
      )
    `);

    // 7. Seed demo operators for all roles
    // Demo Collector (phone: 0300000001, PIN: 1111)

      ON CONFLICT (phone) DO UPDATE SET role='collector', pin='1111', city='Accra', region='Greater Accra'
    `);

    // Demo Aggregator (phone: 0300000002, PIN: 2222)
    await client.query(`

      VALUES ('Green Collect GH', 'Green Collect Ghana Ltd', '0300000002', '2222', 'aggregator', 'Accra', 'Greater Accra', 'Ghana')
      ON CONFLICT (phone) DO UPDATE SET role='aggregator', pin='2222', city='Accra', region='Greater Accra'
    `);

    // Demo Processor = rePATRN (phone: 0300000003, PIN: 3333)
    await client.query(`

      ON CONFLICT (phone) DO UPDATE SET role='processor', pin='3333', city='Tema', region='Greater Accra'
